Current Commentary

Paris Riot Shu 14

France, which had been stable for a long time, although feeling the frenzy of the world economic panic and the threat of fascism, remained safe and stable. On the one hand, it supported the wavering situation of the Treaty of Versailles, and on the other hand, it maintained its position as the leader of European finance, making it impossible for Germany and Italy to ignore the dominance of the French franc. Even the British pound and the US dollar were inevitably affected by it. This was truly no easy task. Unexpectedly, an unexpected incident occurred. A car crash in the suburbs of Paris was originally an accidental event. The Stavisky affair was also not a case related to the general situation of France. But due to a riot in the streets, it became impossible to maintain order, and order was completely broken. The French parliamentary politics are characterized by a proliferation of small parties. There is no lack of right-wing, central, and left-wing parties, such as the Republican Party, the Republican Socialist Party, the Radical Socialist Party, and the Socialist Party. Any one party has at most 150 seats, and it is impossible to have a majority to control the parliament. Therefore, the cabinet based on parliamentary trust is actually unable to implement its so-called democratic politics, and can only organize multi-party cabinets in the form of coalition. The instability of its foundation and the impermanence of its life are already obvious. In the past two years, there have been six changes of cabinets, from Herriot, Boncour, Daladier, Sarraut, Chautemps, and then Daladier again. Most of them are centered on the Socialist and Radical Socialist parties, and none of them have lasted long. This is due to the special situation of the parliament. If the people in power do not have considerable experience, I don't know how many confusions have been brewed.

Since World War I, France's traditional policy has belonged to the category of maintaining the status quo. Therefore, whoever organizes the cabinet, there will be no serious consequences for foreign policy and domestic facilities. But this time, the biggest riot since the Bastille occurred in the city of Paris. The Royalist Party demonstrated everywhere, and the Communist Party counter-demonstrated everywhere. In Paris alone, more than 400 people were killed and injured, and it will spread to important cities such as Lyon and Marseille. Although the Daladier cabinet won a majority of 300 votes in the House of Representatives, it had to resign due to the failure on the streets and the resistance of the masses. The life of the cabinet was only a week, which is also rare. This kind of situation may not have a huge impact on the entire future of France, but parliamentary politics will be even more shaken in the future, which can be foreseen. The performance of the French parliament has also deviated from the masses, and it is difficult to meet the demands of the people, and it is not yet known what path the people will take.

When we examine the future of France, there are three points to pay attention to. (1) The Paris riot is indeed a local political problem within France, but it has a serious impact on the entire French society. It is related to everything in political issues. Will it tend to the right as a result, or not? Its impact can reach all of Europe, causing strong stimulation to international relations, especially to Germany and Italy. It is even more worthy of attention. (2) France's army is arguably the first in Europe, but its population is stagnating. The number of standing soldiers cannot even be filled by French men, and Africans are conscripted. Based on this alone, it is enough to see the difficulties that France cannot easily overcome. (3) Although France has a huge amount of 80 billion francs in cash, it should be able to continue to support its gold standard system, maintain its claims on European countries, and maintain its world dominance in finance. However, within France, it will still be trapped in a stalemate. Low prices and overproduction will eventually become chronic sclerosis. Even the government's budget deficit of 6 billion francs is difficult to fill. Therefore, the general public feels that the burden is too heavy, and the future is also difficult to stabilize.

Japanese Army Launches Threats Towards Russia, 15

Commander of the Hulun Front Warns the Red Army

Minister of the Army Hayashi strengthens the Kwantung Army

(Harbin) Shinohara, the Front Commander of the stationed Hulun unit, issued a warning on the 6th to the Soviet Red Army Commander due to 2,000 members of the Red Jade Mountain volunteer army under the 1st of this month fleeing into Soviet territory.

1. From January 30th to the 1st of this month, around 2,000 armed bandits fled into your country's territory from Manchuria, and it is confirmed that your army has taken them in.

2. Regarding future measures, should anything occur contrary to the friendship between our countries, how greatly the friendship between Manchuria and Russia would be hindered causes me great concern. (Telecommunications Electric, 6th)

(Tokyo) Regarding the expenditures for the Manchurian Incident in the Showa 9 fiscal year, Minister of the Army Hayashi today provided the following explanation at the budget subcommittee regarding the amount exceeding the previous year, including 27,606,394 yen in the regular division and 16,082,264 yen in the temporary division: Due to the operations in Kulunber and Jehol, the defense area of the Kwantung Army has been expanded, and due to various circumstances in the Far East, the strength of the Kwantung Army is being increased to ensure the security of Manchuria and stabilize people's hearts. (Telecommunications Electric, 8th)

(Harbin) The Soviet authorities on the Soviet-Manchurian border last year on November 11th near the village of Oscenson on the banks of the Yam River shelled the mailman Zhang (of the Manchurian state), seizing the postal items and equipment on the boat. It was reported to the head of the Mohe postal office, who filed a serious protest by diplomatic ambassador Shi Lüben to the Soviet consul General Rauts demanding the following three things: 1) severely punish the perpetrators 2) compensate for the damages 3) guarantee that this will not happen again in the future (Telecommunications Electric, 8th)

After Japan's invasion of China,

the world becomes increasingly uneasy 16

Great Britain has a major change in public opinion on disarmament

Expanding armaments becomes increasingly pressing

(London) Yesterday night's discussion in the lower house has shown that disarmament is currently an issue with inconsistent views in British public opinion. Previously, the people of the country almost unanimously believed that disarmament was the most important event in international politics, but today, those who advocate disarmament have mostly changed their opinions, believing that disarmament is indeed necessary, but doubts have arisen as to whether it can actually be implemented. The change in their attitude is, of course, due to the events of the past two years.

Such as Japan's invasion of Manchuria and withdrawal from the League of Nations, Germany's demand for equal armaments and withdrawal from the League of Nations, recent events in Austria, France's attitude towards disarmament, and the United States' resolution to build 120 warships. During the discussion of this matter in the lower house, Baldwin made an important speech, openly declaring the inadequacy of the defense of the British Empire, and Churchill advocated abolishing the London Naval Treaty, which only applies to the United Kingdom, the United States, and Japan, and wanted to greatly increase the British Air Force, because the British Air Force, in terms of numbers, is far inferior to the United States, France, and Russia.

Baldwin said that the British government is making a final effort on the European security issue, so it has submitted a disarmament memorandum. As for whether there is hope of success, it will soon be known. If it fails, then the British government should take responsibility for quickly focusing on British interests first. Even if an agreement is reached, the British government's responsibility lies in ensuring that the United Kingdom actively prepares within the scope permitted by the agreement, striving for efficiency and completeness. This is also what any country must do, because only in this way can it fulfill its responsibilities with other countries when implementing sanctions. (Reuters Electric, 7th)

Japanese attempt to assassinate

British General Allenby 17

The Straits Settlements provide defense funds for Great Britain

(London) British wartime General Lord Allenby traveled to the Far East this past January. While he was in the Dutch East Indies, he returned to England after receiving a secret report of an attempt to harm him. He confirmed upon arriving in London that the assassination plot was discovered. After Allenby arrived in Java, the Dutch authorities suddenly warned him that someone wanted to assassinate him. He does not know the inside story, but he heard that the assassin was an Oriental. It was later learned that he was Japanese, but he does not know the method or the reason. In Singapore, someone suggested that the Straits Settlements should provide 500,000 yuan (approximately 59,000 British pounds) in imperial defense funds. It is said that non-political members will propose this motion when the Legislative Council meets on February 12. (Reuters, 8th)

The Theory of a secret agreement between Japan and Germany

Deputy Speaker of the British Upper House claims to have evidence 18

(Tokyo) According to a Tokyo-based special dispatch from New York, Sir Muller, Deputy Speaker of the British Upper House, declared in New York on the 6th that Japan and Germany have reached a certain understanding regarding Japan's domination, and he has obtained considerable and reliable evidence. He also stated that the recurrence of a world war is extremely frightening. At a time when English-speaking countries are advocating cooperation on the Far Eastern issue, Muller's sudden remarks are noteworthy. (Telecommunications Electric, 8th)

Minister of Commerce Nakajima resigns to take responsibility

Praising Ashikaga Takauji Ten Years Ago 19

Exploiting the Topic, the House of Peers Proposes Impeachment

Matsumoto Joji Succeeds as Minister of Commerce and Industry

(Tokyo) Due to the praise for Ashikaga Takauji, Minister of Commerce and Industry Nakajima, who was in a difficult situation, submitted his resignation at 4:30 PM today. The Prime Minister requested the appointment of Matsumoto Joji, a member of the House of Peers, to succeed him as Minister of Commerce and Industry. (National News Agency, 8th)

(Tokyo) The details of Minister of Commerce and Industry Nakajima's resignation due to the Takauji issue are as follows: Yesterday afternoon, the Minister stated to reporters that he could not advance or retreat based on his personal will. As a result, the overall atmosphere in the House of Peers deteriorated, and a resolution to impeach the government was about to be proposed. The government, seeing this situation, was very flustered and keenly felt the need to take preemptive action. Therefore, at 4:30 PM, Secretary-General Horikiri met with Minister of Commerce and Industry Nakajima, intending to request Nakajima's voluntary decision. Minister of Commerce and Industry Nakajima also knew that the situation had reached this point and submitted his resignation on the grounds of being unable to fulfill his duties due to illness. Secretary-General Horikiri immediately went to Prime Minister Saito's private residence in Yotsuya, delivering Minister of Commerce and Industry Nakajima's resignation in person. The Prime Minister immediately summoned Matsumoto Joji, the former Director-General of the Legislation Bureau, earnestly requesting him to succeed as Minister of Commerce and Industry. After Matsumoto agreed, Nakajima's resignation was conveyed to the Imperial Palace. (Dentsu News Agency, 8th)

(Tokyo) The Ashikaga Takauji issue in the House of Peers developed in a way that the government and most of the House of Peers had not foreseen. Even the Kenkyukai, which held a self-respecting attitude, stated that since the situation had deteriorated so much, Minister of Commerce and Industry Nakajima had no choice but to resign. Although there were criticisms that Mimurodo Keiko (Kenkyukai) had abruptly taken the impeachment out of the scope of questioning the Minister of State, sympathy for Minister of Commerce and Industry Nakajima did not increase as a result. The government had long been at a loss, and some within the government also advocated that the Minister of Commerce and Industry had no choice but to resign, and some cabinet members even argued that Prime Minister Saito, who had recommended the Minister of Commerce and Industry, should also resign due to his responsibility. However, there were also those who said that the problem was the Minister of Commerce and Industry's own problem. When the Saito Cabinet was formed in May of the previous year, Prime Minister Saito could not have foreseen that this problem would arise, and the Minister of Commerce and Industry's essay was written ten years ago, so the Prime Minister could not be held responsible retroactively. Moreover, at this time of emergency, it is especially inappropriate to cause chaos in the overall situation. Therefore, although the Minister of Commerce and Industry's resignation is unavoidable, the government should be cautious. (Dentsu News Agency, 8th)

(Tokyo) Regarding the Takauji issue of Minister of Commerce and Industry Nakajima in the House of Peers, the government initially thought it was not optimistic, but ultimately Minister of Commerce and Industry Nakajima resigned due to this. In the plenary session on the 7th, Viscount Mimurodo pressed Prime Minister Saito to recommend the Minister of Commerce and Industry and vigorously pursued answers. In the plenary session on the 8th, the government still did not answer and postponed it to the plenary session on the 9th. The government was concerned that the Prime Minister's response would cause serious consequences, so it carefully reviewed the verbatim record of the 8th and examined in detail the questions asked by Viscount Mimurodo. At the same time, it was discussed in detail at the cabinet seats in the House of Peers. However, from the government's standpoint, the Prime Minister could only insist on expressing regret, or perhaps separate the responsibility of recommending the Minister of Commerce and Industry from the Minister of Commerce and Industry's writing disaster, making it a completely separate issue. It is said that the government will base its response on this strategy. (Nikkan News Agency, 8th)

(Tokyo) The newly appointed Minister of Commerce and Industry, Dr. Matsumoto Joji, is from Gifu Prefecture, born in Meiji 10 (1877), and is currently 58 years old. He was a professor at the Imperial University and holds a doctorate in law. He is an authority in the business world. Later, he was involved with the South Manchuria Railway for many years and was also the Director-General of the Legislation Bureau of the Kiyoura Cabinet. He has served as a member of the House of Peers and has been a lawyer for a long time, a leading figure in that field. His name has been frequently mentioned whenever a cabinet is formed, and his knowledge and personality are considered to be those of a capable minister. The general public is pleased that he has been appointed as Minister of Commerce and Industry this time. (Nikkan News Agency, 8th)

Page 8

Shinpo Second Edition (8)

The Daladier Government Dies Young

Doumergue Receives Mandate to Form Cabinet 20

Conditional on Dissolving Parliament

The Public Is Won Over; Old but Vigorous

Recruiting Prominent Figures to Form a Strong Government

Individuals Involved in Corruption Cases Are Generally Excluded from the Cabinet

(Paris) As angry crowds across Paris shouted (revenge), the short-lived Daladier cabinet died yesterday. After several hours of hesitation, the 70-year-old former President Doumergue agreed to take the premiership.

After Doumergue accepted the mandate to form a cabinet, the political situation began to clear. It is widely believed that the new cabinet will recruit several prominent figures and may be formed within twelve hours. Doumergue's acceptance was compelled by the earnest persuasion of President Lebrun, and both the Senate, Chamber of Deputies, and members of the Paris City Council supported it. Doumergue, who originally lived in the countryside, immediately packed his bags and came to Beijing after agreeing to form a cabinet. Doumergue's first action after taking office was to issue an order that all national theaters would be closed last night to show the nation's condolences for the victims. Previously, the President had summoned Barthou (who served as Prime Minister from 1910 to 1913) to the presidential residence for consultation, and then decided to ask Doumergue to bear the burden, as Doumergue had initially declined. (Reuters, 8th)

Former President Doumergue arrived in Paris at 8:30 this morning, after leaving his private residence in Turneville. A large crowd gathered at the station, shouting "Long Live Doumergue" and "Long Live France." In less than two minutes, Doumergue entered the presidential palace to formally accept the mandate to form a cabinet from President Lebrun, and immediately consulted with key political figures. He also visited the speakers of the Senate and Chamber of Deputies. So far, Doumergue has consistently refused to issue a statement to reporters, so the new cabinet's lineup is currently unknown. As Doumergue's car passed through the streets, it became the target of cheers from the people of Paris, who expressed their trust in him. (Havas, 8th)

(Paris) Paris has returned to normal after the riots of the past two days. According to veteran politicians, the 71-year-old former President intends to organize a new cabinet whose members have no connection to the Bayonne affair or other political and financial corruption cases, and who are trusted not only by the Parliament but also by the entire French people. (National News Agency, 8th)

(Paris) There is speculation that Caillaux, who previously served as Prime Minister and Finance Minister, may be appointed as the new Finance Minister. Théodore, Herriot, and Barthou are all expected to join the cabinet. (Reuters, 8th)

The Founding Father Takes on a Difficult Task

Unanimous Support from All Parties 21

No One but Him Can Be the Pillar

The Nation Is in Trouble; Stop Partisan Strife

The New Cabinet Lacks a Solid Foundation Due to a Lack of Party Discipline

Will Avoid Dissolving Parliament Unless Absolutely Necessary

(Paris) Members of the Senate and Chamber of Deputies, and former Prime Ministers of all political colors, support Doumergue's formation of a cabinet. Even Herriot, the leader of the Radical Socialist Party and former Prime Minister, with the consent of his party, is also among those in support. Members of the Radical Socialist Party and other parties held separate meetings in the afternoon. Doumergue will not encounter major difficulties in forming a cabinet tomorrow. The cabinet he forms will be a kind of "truce cabinet of all parties." The official gazette released by the presidential palace in the evening stated that former President Doumergue, at the urging of President Lebrun, and with a psychology of complete loyalty to the country, will take on the difficult task. In addition, members of the Senate and Chamber of Deputies who have served as Prime Minister also issued a public statement after a meeting, saying that at this time of national crisis, no one can be a stronger pillar than former President Doumergue. Therefore, the whole body unanimously expressed sympathy for Doumergue's cabinet formation and notified Doumergue of this intention. The public statement also said that while they have made this expression, they are not imposing any restrictions on Doumergue's actions, and Doumergue is completely free to select cabinet members. (Havas, 7th)

(Paris) All of France's most powerful political parties, except the Socialist Party, have agreed to support Doumergue, at least as far as their leaders are concerned. The new cabinet may recruit former Prime Ministers. It is said that the new cabinet lacks genuine unity and party discipline, so its foundation is as weak as previous cabinets. Although the Parliament is the most difficult obstacle to overcome, Doumergue will still do his best to manipulate the various parties in the Chamber of Deputies to avoid resorting to dissolution. This is common in other countries, but in France, it is not done unless absolutely necessary. In the past sixty years, it has only been done once. Doumergue, because party governments have repeatedly failed, now intends to organize a government of national unity, but ultimately cannot be tainted with the colors of the Radical Socialist Party and the Socialist Party. These two parties are no longer trusted in the eyes of the voters. However, the two parties are deeply concerned about the rise of the fascist Tittoni and fear that the semi-dictator Chapu will seize power with the help of the royalists, so they will temporarily put aside their actions. Many people believe that the only solution now lies in reforming civil administration, providing appropriate compensation, and breaking away from political bias. The responsibility for preserving the French Third Republic now rests with Doumergue. Doumergue, commonly known as "Papa," has become the most beloved person in the country. Doumergue retired from political life and married in his hometown after his term as President from 1924 to 1931. Doumergue is the first Christian to serve as President of France. (Reuters, 8th)

Doumergue's Conditions for Forming a Cabinet

Retain the Right to Dissolve Parliament 22

(Paris) It is widely rumored in political circles that Doumergue's acceptance of the mandate to form a cabinet is conditional not only on dissolving parliament and at least postponing the general election for six months, but also on advocating amending the constitution and reinstating the Paris Police Chief Chiappe. If the President accepts these conditions, Doumergue can govern for at least half a year without interference from parliament. The President has ordered Chamber of Deputies Speaker Bouisson to contact the leaders of various parties and invite them to join the new cabinet. Bouisson consulted with Daladier, Chautemps, Tittoni, and Herriot last night, but the results are unknown. (National News Agency, 7th)

(Paris) One of the shortcomings of the French constitution is that it is extremely difficult to dissolve parliament, which is the main reason for the current political turmoil. Since 1871, the President has only used his privilege to announce the dissolution of parliament once. According to the Paris Echo, after the previous Chautemps cabinet fell, former President Doumergue declined current President Lebrun's invitation to take the premiership, not because of his age, but because President Lebrun was unwilling to fulfill two conditions: dissolving parliament and postponing the general election for six months. However, this matter has made those who advocate for a major reform of the constitution even more vocal. (National News Agency, 7th)

Two Days of Storm and Waves

Paris Gradually Calming Down 23

Frenzied Crowds Turn to Welcome Former President

Special Alert Lifted This Morning

(Paris) After a storm, France is calm this morning, and everyone has a pleasant feeling, believing that someone has come forward in time to clean up the crisis. The only thing in Paris that still indicates that life has not returned to normal is the delayed delivery of the first batch of mail, as the post office is still occupied by soldiers for defense. Former President Doumergue, who has agreed to form a new cabinet, is welcomed by the crowds as if he were a beloved monarch. When Doumergue drove to the presidential palace, those who saw him along the way smiled and paid their respects. The crowds, who were frenzied with anger yesterday, have transformed today into cheering and applauding. In addition to police protection along the way, a squadron of cavalry escorted Doumergue. Doumergue talked with the President for half an hour and then began the political considerations necessary for forming a cabinet. Only ten members of the Chamber of Deputies arrived this morning, so the meeting was adjourned after only two minutes, until after the new cabinet is formed. At the same time, the municipal government hired people to quickly clear the debris from the streets. Paris is gradually calming down after Daladier's resignation, so the special alert measures were lifted at 1:45 this morning. Although the disturbances last night were not as serious as on Tuesday, there was still bloodshed. According to the Paris Morning News, three people died and many were injured after armed demonstrators clashed with police, and many were arrested. It is reported that the demonstration led by the Communist Party was the most violent. Furthermore, last night's demonstration was different from the previous night because the previous night was a national movement, while last night was the work of a few parties. Many troublemakers participated last night, resulting in looting. (Reuters, 8th)

Daladier Hangs Up His Hat

Popular Grievances Boil Over; He Resigns 24

Leaves the Presidential Palace with a Pale Face

Daladier conferred at the Presidential Palace for many hours on Tuesday night, and it was not until dawn that he emerged, with a serious but also haggard face. He then issued an order to increase the number of troops to supplement the inadequacy of the 14,000 police officers. However, after seeing the boiling popular grievances, he announced his resignation. Opposition members of parliament blamed Daladier for ordering the police to fire on the crowds. Unfortunately, Daladier held the premiership for a very short time and personally heard the demonstrators shouting slogans to drive him out. The mob shouted wildly, "Resign, resign," and sometimes even shouted, "Kill him." What was especially unpleasant was the cry of "We also have weapons. We know what we should do now." (Reuters, 8th)

(Paris) The following is a report on the situation before and after the resignation of the Daladier cabinet. Prime Minister Daladier held a meeting this morning with Chamber of Deputies Speaker Puisson, Radical Socialist Party leader Herriot, Socialist Party leaders Blum and Frossard, right-wing member of parliament Ibanez, Minister of the Army Pengu, and Minister of the Navy Chappetellan. Following this, at 1:15 PM, he went to the presidential palace to meet with President Lebrun and submit the cabinet's collective resignation. A quarter of an hour later, Daladier came out and issued a public statement to the press, saying, "The government is responsible for public safety, but in the current situation, order cannot be maintained without taking extraordinary measures. The cabinet cannot bear to use troops to suppress the demonstrating masses and stage another bloody tragedy, so the whole body has resigned to the President." The resigning cabinet continued to meet from 2:00 PM to 5:30 PM to study the current situation, with particular emphasis on the responsibility for maintaining public safety before the establishment of a new cabinet. This morning, Ishii, the Secretary-General of the National Federation of Trade Unions, visited Daladier and did not agree with the cabinet's resignation, saying that he reserved the freedom of personal action in order to cope with future events. Cabinet members were very concerned about Ishii's visit to the Prime Minister. People in the trade union explained Ishii's words as a sign that the National Federation of Trade Unions would take severe action against pan-fascism. The Mine Workers' Union also sent a representative to visit Daladier, with the same tone as the representative of the National Federation of Trade Unions. (Havas, 7th)

Viewpoints of French and British Newspapers

Daladier Retires Courageously 25

Still Admirable and Upright

French Democratic Politics Are Deeply Rooted

Amending the Constitution Seems Unlikely

(Paris) All newspapers believe that Daladier's resignation of the cabinet will ease people's hearts at this time of popular anger. Le Petit Parisien said, "Daladier did not want to use troops to suppress the masses and stage another bloody tragedy, so he hung up his hat and left. His actions were admirable and upright, and we cannot accuse him of showing weakness." Most newspapers agree with Daladier's resignation, but the rhetoric of the left and right newspapers is different. The Socialist Party's "People's Daily" blamed "Daladier for yielding to the threats of the reactionaries." Right-wing newspapers fiercely attacked Daladier and Interior Minister Frot, saying that they were driven out by public opinion. The crowd sees former President Doumergue's appointment as prime minister as the only way to stabilize people's hearts, but the Socialist Party's "People's Daily" does not think so. "L'Écho de Paris" greatly praised Doumergue, saying, "Former President Doumergue is widely expected, and in this time of national difficulty, he will unite people's hearts and support the overall situation, a responsibility that no one else can bear." "Le Journal" also praised Doumergue, saying, "Since Tiger Prime Minister Clemenceau, no politician has been more loved by the people than Doumergue. The factional disputes in the Chamber of Deputies have plunged the country into its current situation. If Doumergue can come out of the mountain, the public will be convinced, and the disputes will naturally cease." The Radical Party's "L'Ère Nouvelle" said that dissolving the Chamber of Deputies is a political means commonly used by the United Kingdom, and Doumergue is afraid that he will not take this path. Judging from the current situation and people's hearts, France cannot but organize an authoritarian government, and no one is better suited to be the leader of an authoritarian government than Doumergue. Doumergue's cabinet will be supported by the vast majority from the day it is established. (Havas, 8th)

(London) British newspapers are very supportive of the news that former French President Doumergue has been mandated to form a cabinet. For example, the Manchester Guardian said that the world knows that Doumergue is a great French-style politician, and that he will be able to combine the Radical and Central factions to form a new cabinet and maintain cooperation between the various parties, as this is what is needed at the moment. The Times said that dissolving parliament is not allowed by French political convention, and France will continue to strive to maintain democratic politics. Therefore, although extreme right-wingers advocate changing the constitutional mechanism, it is doubtful whether it will become a reality. The Daily Telegraph also holds the same view, saying that it is impossible for France to allow the Fascist or Communist parties to seize the life of the government and change course. However, the Daily Mail, which has recently changed its attitude and advocated fascism, criticized the French democratic system. (Havas, 8th)

The Goal of Overthrowing the Cabinet Has Been Achieved

The Mob's Remaining Anger Has Not Subsided 26

Wanting to Get Frot to Be Satisfied

Lawyers Demand Expulsion from Membership

The most important goal of the rioters was to overthrow Daladier, but although the goal has been achieved, the remaining anger has not subsided, and the streets are still full of danger. Interior Minister Frot is the most hated by the people, and they will not be satisfied until they get him. Four hundred lawyers have formed a team to go to the Ministry of Justice to demand that the president of the bar expel Frot from the legal profession. (Reuters, 8th)

(Paris) This afternoon, the courts here were noisy. More than 100 lawyers formed a group and asked the president of the bar association to expel the resigning Interior Minister Frot from the association. Although the president tried to persuade them to calm down, the lawyers still held a demonstration, singing the national anthem in front of Frot's lawyer uniform and burning the uniform. After the news of the cabinet's resignation spread, crowds of people gathered on the streets and sang the national anthem. (Havas, 7th)

Demonstrations in the Streets

A Chorus of Revenge 27

Rumors Abound; People Are Uneasy

Near Midnight; The Disturbance Gradually Subsides

Street gatherings are prohibited. But as soon as it was afternoon, crowds gathered on the Place de la Concorde, and the police dispersed them. They scattered and gathered again, and some people threw sharp objects at the police, shouting, "We will bring our guns tonight."

In the afternoon, crowds marched through the major streets, singing the Marseillaise, and sometimes clashed with the police. Before long, cavalry galloped through the Place de la Concorde to clear the gathering crowds. In view of the fact that rioters set fires on Tuesday, the naval headquarters stationed troops at key points outside the building to guard it.

A group of rioters assaulted Senator Roland in the Rue Royale, tearing his clothes, because Roland had ordered troops and patrol teams to fire on Tuesday night in order to protect the government. Roland hurriedly boarded a streetcar, but was rescued by the police before he could escape. In the evening, crowds gathered again on the Place de la Concorde, and the situation was more serious than in the afternoon. The cries of "Revenge," "Revenge" did not stop, and they attacked the Republican Guard. The members of the group had no choice but to push and chase several times, resulting in two injuries. The casualties of the rioters must be far greater than this number.

In the evening, Paris Police Chief Chiappe decided to provide helmets to the police to ensure their safety. Although rumors were rife throughout the city and the police were very nervous, everything was still easy to control, and there were no casualties. However, the helmeted police teams injured many people when they pushed and chased the demonstrating crowds at the intersection of Place de la Concorde and Rue de la Madeleine. The crowds insulted and abused the police, threw sharp objects, and destroyed street lamps and windows. They also lit torches along the major streets to cheer them on. At 10:30 PM, Rue de Rivoli was very quiet, and the Place de la Concorde was also quieter with 1,000 police officers stationed there. In the recent disturbances, in addition to injuring many civilians, 10 police officers were injured, and hundreds of people were arrested. Near midnight, there were occasional gunshots on the major streets, but by 1:00 this morning, everything was quiet. The Communist Party attempted to dig trenches somewhere and resist the police with pistols, but they were disarmed and arrested. The Veterans Association and the Jeunesse Patriotes, the two main groups in the Tuesday riots, were warned by their leaders not to stage any more demonstrations. (Reuters, 8th)

More Than Three Hundred People Arrested

To Be Charged with Treason 28

Estimated Results of the Conflict

More Than Four Hundred Seriously and Lightly Injured

It is reported that a total of about 350 people were arrested, including the veteran reporter Muras of L'Action Française. The people will be charged with treason, arson, and inciting murder. The newspaper issued by L'Action Française yesterday was confiscated in its entirety. L'Action Française reporter Muras was briefly questioned at the police station and then released.

Three members of the city guard, who were initially thought to have been thrown into the Seine River by the mob, were found in the hospital, but they were covered in injuries.

The city police chief was seriously injured when he clashed with rioters at the intersection of Rue de la Madeleine at midnight and was rushed to the hospital for emergency treatment. (Reuters, 8th)

As a result of the clashes in various places, several police officers were injured. The number of civilians injured is difficult to calculate. There were two deaths and many arrests. Except for four people whose cases were more serious and who have been detained, the rest were released soon. According to the Paris Police Chief's estimate, about 2,000-3,000 people marched on the streets tonight. According to official statistics, 10 people died and 182 people were sent to the hospital for treatment as a result of last night's disturbance. The remaining 282 people were slightly injured. (Havas, 7th)

Stock Exchange Ceases Work

A Memorial to the Victims 29

Wild Cries of "Kill Daladier" Unceasing

Police Smile and Stand by

The employees of the stock exchange stopped working at 1:45 PM, shouting "Send Daladier to the guillotine" and "Murderer" without stopping. More and more people gathered in the exchange. Several police officers leaned against the wall and listened to the public cries with smiles. After a while, the illuminated message board revealed the numbers "Daladier has resigned." Then, cheers erupted throughout the venue. After a short while, the venue returned to calm, and the staff resumed work as usual.

When the stock exchange opened yesterday, thousands of people gathered, shouting "Kill Daladier" and "Long Live Chauvin," making it impossible to carry out transactions. The police could not maintain order, and the police station requested reinforcements. But although a large number of police officers came by car to help, they were unable to drive them out because there were too many people in the exchange. In order to commemorate those who were killed last night, the stock exchange made a five-minute silence and wrote in large letters on the blackboard, "Five minutes of silence for the victims." (Reuters, 8th)

Chaotic Scenes in Paris

Sufficient to Show the Fierceness of the Riot 30

Almost No Gas Lamps Are Intact

Leaking Gas Sprays Flames Like Firebrands

Today, looking at the scenes on several major streets, one can imagine the fierceness of Tuesday and yesterday's riots. Nineteen newspaper racks were destroyed and burned. No gas lamps are intact in the Rue du Faubourg-Montmartre, and countless gas mains were destroyed. The leaking gas sprayed flames like firebrands in the London fog. A Reuters interviewer walked on the Boulevard des Capucines and saw a communist shot in the abdomen, lying on the sidewalk. Two other people fired at the police.

At night, countless private cars carrying women in evening dresses slowly drove through the city. They were terrified by the sight of the mob and police clashing and the streets littered with broken objects.

One of Paris's most fashionable cafes presented a strange scene rarely seen on weekdays. One part gathered customers in tattered clothes with angry faces, while the other part sat diners in elegant evening clothes, calmly eating. (Reuters, 8th)

The Paris General Confederation of Labour Announces

General Strike Next Monday 31

Oppose Fascism

Protect the Freedom of the People

(Paris) The General Confederation of Labor today ordered a twenty-four-hour general strike on Monday to protest the encroachment of Fascists and to protect the freedom of the people. Postal workers have announced their willingness to join the strike. Meanwhile, a delegation from the Veterans Federation visited President Lebrun, presenting a unanimously passed resolution opposing the authorities' actions of injuring and killing peaceful demonstrators, and requesting the dissolution of Parliament and the formation of a strong and honest government composed of individuals respected by the people. Otherwise, the action that angered the people on Tuesday will cause former soldiers without weapons to return to the streets, and next time they will bring hand grenades. (8th National Telegram)

Cordial Talks Between Austria and Hungary

Maintain Coordination in Political and Economic Matters 32

Date for Austria's Appeal to the League of Nations Undetermined

Budapest. Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss has arrived here on a visit to the Hungarian authorities. He met with Prime Minister Gömbös for two hours and then met with Foreign Minister Kánya to begin discussing general diplomatic issues. In the evening, the government authorities hosted a banquet for Dollfuss. They delivered speeches to each other, which were extremely cordial. Dollfuss said in his reply, "The friendship between Austria and Hungary is so profound that there is no need to conclude any treaties or conventions. At present, the international community is adopting a policy of 'convention inflation,' and we have no need to follow suit. The sincerity of economic cooperation between Austria and Hungary is far more valuable than any convention." (8th Havas Telegram)

Budapest, Hungary. After negotiations between the Austrian and Hungarian Prime Ministers, a joint communiqué was issued stating that the two leaders had a coordinated spirit on all political and economic issues between the two countries, and the results of the negotiations were satisfactory. Prime Minister Dollfuss also declared separately to the press that relations between Austria and Hungary had never been as satisfactory as they are today. He also said that rumors outside that the Austrian government was about to collapse were completely unfounded, and that he was determined to defend the people and would vigorously prevent disruptive elements. (8th Havas Telegram)

(Geneva) The Austrian State Council will hold a meeting next Saturday to decide in principle to seek direct recourse to the League of Nations regarding the Austro-German conflict, but the date has not yet been determined. Today, the Austrian representative to the League of Nations, Pflügl, visited the Secretary-General of the League of Nations, Avenol, to inform him of the steps that the Austrian government intends to take in the future. For Reciprocal Visit to Moscow 33

And to Explain the New German-Polish Agreement

Warsaw. Because of differing interpretations in the Soviet Union regarding the non-aggression pact concluded between Germany and Poland, Foreign Minister Colonel Beck has decided to personally go to Moscow on the 12th of this month to provide an explanation in person, in order to prove that although Poland has established a new relationship with Germany, its friendship with neighboring countries and allies remains unchanged. (7th Havas Telegram)

Balkan Pact

Formal Signing Today 34

Bulgarian Prime Minister Declares Support for Peace

But Will Not Abandon Rights Recognized by the League of Nations

Capital of Yugoslavia. The Balkan Pact negotiated by the Balkan countries is scheduled to be formally signed in the capital of Greece this Friday. It is reported that Romania, Yugoslavia, Turkey, and Greece, the four contracting states, have decided to make slight revisions to the text of the treaty after exchanging opinions. (7th Havas Telegram)

Sofia. The Prime Minister of Bulgaria recently issued a statement to the press, stating that after other Balkan countries studied Bulgaria's proposal to sign a non-aggression treaty, although they considered the Balkan Pact to be more sufficient to ensure the security of the Balkan countries, the four Balkan countries are still prepared to sign a non-aggression treaty. It can be seen that Bulgaria is deeply willing to express its support for peace. The Bulgarian government has never wanted to modify the boundaries defined by the treaty by force. He then mentioned Bulgaria's attitude towards the Balkan Pact, saying that this kind of pact is useless, and his conclusion was: "On the day before the formal signing of the Balkan Pact, we will notify the League of Nations and the signatory countries of the Pact of our views. What are our views? We refuse to sign the Balkan Pact. This is because we are willing to maintain peace, and we cannot abandon the rights recognized by the League of Nations Covenant." (Note: This should refer to Article 19 of the League of Nations Covenant, "Review of Treaties Which Have Become Inapplicable"), etc.

The Waterway Management Association Plans

To Dredge the Yangtze River Waterway 48

(Nanjing) The Yangtze River's water depletion last winter was unprecedented in decades. The ships traveling upstream were either suspended or stranded. According to the Yangtze River Waterway Management Association, the Yangtze River has been gradually silted up in recent years, especially in the Madang area. If it is past the autumn flood season, the water will rise strangely, and in the winter, the water will be strangely shallow. Therefore, dredging the Yangtze River waterway is an urgent matter. It will cost 60 million yuan to manage the entire river. It is now planned to start in stages, first dredging the waterway upstream and downstream of Madang, where the silting is the most severe. The measurement has been completed, and it will cost about two to three million yuan. It is requested that the Economic Commission allocate the funds from the cotton and wheat loan. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Yellow River Flood Relief Committee has formulated three fund-raising measures: 1. Imitate the previous breach method and implement a surcharge on railways, telecommunications, and ships. 2. The governments of the relevant provinces shall designate appropriate guarantees, such as land tax, to issue bonds for the post-disaster engineering of the Yellow River breach. 3. Please ask the National Economic Commission to rush to allocate cotton and wheat loans, which will be submitted to the Central Political Council for decision soon. (8th Special Dispatch)

The original telegram is as follows: (Titles omitted) It is hereby announced that by order of the Executive Yuan, regarding the commendation ceremony for the Dalai Lama's passing, it was instructed to hold a memorial service in Nanjing, etc. The Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission was instructed to work with relevant departments to jointly organize the Preparatory Office for the Memorial Service to make proper preparations, etc. After the first preparatory meeting, it was decided that the memorial service would be held on the 14th of this month. The address of the Preparatory Office is within the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission. The address of the Memorial Service is at the Examination Yuan's examination hall. All the above items have been submitted for approval. The office was officially established on the 6th of this month. If any units outside of Nanjing send personnel to Nanjing to pay respects, please telegraph in advance. If you wish to send gifts, please also send them directly to this office for transfer. Apart from detailed arrangements to be announced in newspapers, this telegram is specially sent. Preparatory Office for the Dalai Lama's Memorial Service, respectfully. Administrative Court

Receives Many Cases of Petition 75

(Nanjing) The Administrative Court receives an average of more than sixty cases of petition each month. Some are because the nature of the cases belongs to the scope of impeachment by the Control Yuan. Some are because the procedures are incomplete (must be tried by the court first, and then the petition can be filed with the court if not satisfied). Some are because the written petitions are not in the correct format (must use the court's form; ordinary court forms are not acceptable). All three of these must be rejected. Therefore, on average, only more than thirty petition cases can be established each month. After a petition case is recognized by the court, the court will notify the official agency being petitioned to respond. If the original petitioner still believes that the official agency is unreasonable, they can argue again. As a result, if the official agency is in the wrong and the court makes a ruling, the court will submit it to the Judicial Yuan and then to the National Government to legally punish the official agency being petitioned. If the people suffer losses, the official agency must be responsible for compensation. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

A Comparison of the Military Quality of Russian and Japanese Troops (Vladivostok Correspondence) 107

The national defense of the Soviet Union can be boasted about to the world. However, on the other hand, I The Far East problem I reveals a terrible crisis, which is the seriousness of the Soviet-Japanese problem. From an optimistic perspective, the outstanding issues between the Soviet Union and Japan, such as the dispute over the North Pacific fishing grounds and the oil problem, have been temporarily resolved. Only the China Eastern Railway remains a major case spanning there.

According to the opinions expressed by the main persons in charge of the Soviet Union, if Japanese imperialism continues to run rampant and dares to invade Soviet territory, then the Soviet Union will never back down at that time and will rise up to fight. According to observations of the situation here, Japan has not made any special representations on this, except that the Asahikawa 7th Division will be transferred to Manchuria, and a part of the Hirosaki 8th Division will be transferred back to Japan. In total, the Japanese troops stationed along the China Eastern Railway consist of the entire 10th Division, the entire 7th Division, an artillery brigade, and two cavalry brigades, totaling about 60,000 people. In addition, there are the 14th Division in South Manchuria, a part of the 20th Division in Korea, six garrison battalions, a part of the 6th Division, and other special forces, totaling about 140,000 people. On the Soviet side, from Chita to Vladivostok, in addition to the two Pacific Fleets, the 35th and 36th Army Corps, and special forces, there are only 120,000 to 130,000 people in total. However, their combat power is very strong, and there are plenty of new weapons. Moreover, the Soviet side emphasizes defense and has no intention of actively attacking.

Now, let's make a comparison of the military quality of the Soviet and Japanese troops, which can also give a glimpse into the future trend of war between the Soviet Union and Japan.

The source of Soviet troops and the conscription system are the same as those of other countries, all coming from the people, especially selected from among workers and peasants. The term of service is two years. Military training is not much different from that of various land armies. Those habits of the Tsarist era have been completely eradicated. What is particularly special, and what no other country has, is political training. Needless to say, every soldier can understand his mission in wartime. │In the Tsarist era, they may have understood, but not very clearly, and there were many personal hobbies, such as drinking, which were enough to affect their combat power. │Now it is different. In addition to strict and effective military training, there is also a political understanding. They know their mission, they know why they want to fight their enemies.

In the Japanese army, military training is of course very thorough and meticulous. It is no stronger than any excellent land army country in the world. In terms of military action, the Red Army is still inferior to it, because the national education tradition of the Japanese military has penetrated deeply into the hearts of the people, so ordinary soldiers can faithfully fulfill their mission. However, they have not paid sufficient attention to politics, and it can even be said that there is no political training, which leads to the following two major shortcomings. First, the level of knowledge in Japan has gradually increased, and the research of social sciences is not entirely a temporary fashion, but is gradually penetrating into the lower masses of the general society. The Japanese soldiers come from the people, they have already recognized reality, and the idea of ​​unease has spread throughout the minds of the general public. Therefore, the effectiveness of anesthetics such as loyalty to the emperor and love of the country has indeed been very small. Mechanical oppression can still be maintained in peacetime. Small wars and short periods can still be sustained. Once faced with a major war, I am afraid that changes will occur.

Second, there is the implication of life eviction. Conscription is nothing more than picking and choosing among workers and peasants. During periods of stable life, they can still reluctantly devote themselves to the country and expand their territory to create a better living environment. But now, Japanese villages are on the verge of bankruptcy. The parents, wives, and children of ordinary soldiers and even lower-ranking officers are miserable on the poverty line, not knowing where their next meal will come from. Cities are also encountering a great economic depression, and the difficulties of life are very serious. Therefore, patriotic thoughts are fundamentally shaken. If there is a real long-term war, who can guarantee that they will not change? (Vladivostok, January 27)

Beiping Military Branch

Steps After Removal of Sun's Position 108

Order Sun's troops to be under the command of Yu Shiming

Send Guan and Liu's divisions to assist in attacking Sun's troops

Urge Shanxi's Yan to dispatch troops to assist Nanjing

Beiping Correspondence: He Yingqin, Chairman of the Beiping Military Branch, issued an order yesterday (the 5th) to strip Sun Dianying of his position as commander of the 41st Army and commander of the 40th Division, and telegraphed the Military Commission and the Executive Yuan. All of Sun's troops were placed under the command of Yu Shiming, Ding Futing, and Liu Yueting. Fearing that Sun's troops would still advance westward, He Yingqin invited the generals of North China to the Jurentang last night for discussions on how to deal with Sun's troops. The results decided: (1) If Sun Dianying does not hand over military power and resists the orders of the Military Branch, it is decided to jointly dispatch troops from the five provinces of Shanxi, Suiyuan, Gansu, Ningxia, and Qinghai to encircle and suppress him in accordance with the previous plan to thoroughly resolve the issue. (2) Hou Cheng will be sent to Shanxi to meet with Yan, urging the troops of Shanxi and Suiyuan provinces to dispatch troops to the border between Ningxia and Suiyuan to tail Sun's troops and discuss with Yan the passage of large troops through Shanxi and Suiyuan provinces. (3) When necessary, send the entire division of Guan Linzheng and the cavalry regiment of Liu Duoquan's division to assist, opening the Ping-Sui Railway to concentrate in Baotou, and contact the Shanxi-Suiyuan army to attack Dengkou and the Yellow River bend. According to official sources, Sun's troops aimed to occupy Ningxia and drive westward. When Sun's troops set out, his subordinates suggested to Sun that going to the northwest via Ningxia would definitely be blocked by Ma's army. It would be best to advance southwest of the Yellow River bend without passing through the border of Ningxia to avoid obstacles along the way. After arriving in Woye, they should take a single breath and rush through Ningxia. Sun, because Ma Hongkui had previously telegraphed to obstruct his westward advance, was quite angry. Therefore, he told those who made suggestions that his purpose was to overwhelm Ma Hongkui before advancing westward. Therefore, he did not adopt the suggestion to avoid marching through the border of Ningxia and advanced from various places such as Chengkou and Ligangbu, confronting Ma's army for more than 20 days. Most of Ma's reinforcements have arrived. In recent days, the war on the front line has been fierce, the most intense since the conflict began. Because the authorities dismissed Sun Dianying from his positions, he was bound to take risks and planned to occupy Ningxia in the shortest possible time. If the combined forces of Gansu, Ningxia, and Qinghai are too strong to resist, he will advance westward along the border of Ningxia via the Mongolian border. If Ningxia's strength is insufficient to resist, he will occupy Ningxia and then observe the situation and continue to advance westward. He did not respond to He Yingqin's telegram of the 5th.

After Sun Dianying was dismissed, his main force is still gathered north of the capital of Ningxia Province, launching fierce attacks on the city walls from time to time. According to Guihua telegram, the defending army of Ningxia is Zhan's brigade of Ma Hongkui's troops. Sun's army encircled about 15,000 people. Pingluo was indeed occupied by Sun's army. Ma Baolin, the brigade commander defending Pingluo, was killed in action. About 4,000 people were wiped out and killed in a terrible massacre. A small unit of Sun's army, Yang Hou, was blown up by a landmine, killing more than 700 people. Yan Xishan once sent Councilor Chen Jiashen to Suiyuan to investigate the situation of the Sun-Ma war and has now returned to Bing to report. However, tonight the Military Branch officially denied the loss of Pingluo and announced a telegram from Ningxia stating that the troops from Gansu and Qinghai provinces had actively reinforced the capital of Ningxia Province and that Ma Hongkui's troops inside the city were prepared to launch a major counterattack. The Military Branch will not issue an order to suppress Sun's army because it has sent Yu Shiming and others to take charge of the reorganization. If the army resists, it will be jointly attacked by the five provinces of Shanxi, Suiyuan, Gansu, Ningxia, and Qinghai.

Yan Xishan's attitude is quite noteworthy, because Suiyuan borders Ningxia, and Suiyuan is defended by the Shanxi army. If Yan is consistent with the central government, Sun's army will be easily resolved. It is heard that after authorities here sent representatives to negotiate with Yan repeatedly, Yan has expressed his consistency with the central government and decided to send Wang Jingguo's 70th Division and Zhao Chengzhou's cavalry division to assist Ningxia. Once they receive the dispatch fees from the central government, they can mobilize. However, Yan's attitude has always been mysterious, and the actual issues still need to be discussed in detail. (4th)

Entering Fujian

Various Armies Ordered to Demobilize 109

Fourth Route Army Returns to East Road Control

Jiang and Wei to Immediately Take New Positions on East Road

Fuzhou Correspondence: The 19th Route Army in the Xingquan area has been reorganized by the central government. A few have retreated to Longyan, and scattered soldiers are being pacified separately. Seventh Route Established

Office in Guangdong 110

Sichuan Army

Bloody Battle of Madu Pass 111

Xu Bandit Shoots Commander, Soldiers Mutiny

Government Troops Take Advantage of the Situation to Attack and Capture Strategic Pass

Chongqing Communication: In Sichuan, the military campaign to suppress bandits, since the complete recovery of the five counties of Xuan, Sui, Ying, Peng, and Yi, has completed more than two-thirds of its work. Recently, the battle of Madu Pass was very fierce, with both sides advancing and retreating seven or eight times. Furthermore, because the Xu bandit was tyrannical by nature, he blamed the loss of the pass (the strategic Madu Pass) on Zhang, the commander of his Ninth Army, and shot him. The entire bandit division mutinied. Government troops took advantage of the situation to brave the snow and launch a fierce attack, climbing vines and ropes, using strength as ladders, and climbing up. Finally, they recovered Madu Pass, the only natural barrier between Tong, Ba, Xuan, and Sui. The success was due to the infighting among the bandits and the fierce advance taken advantage of. This matter is rarely known to outsiders. It was later confessed by surrendered prisoners, which is highly credible. Therefore, it is recorded in detail below.

Attacking High Mountains 112

After the Fifth Route Army occupied Majia Chang, it worked hard to advance. When the 7th Brigade of the unit reached Hujia Chang, the Red bandits immediately retreated from the front. The Fifth Route Army continued to occupy Dadongzhai, Maoheshan, Yanwoshan, Chajianci, Luogushan, Jigongliang, Hongya, and various other large mountains, about 1200 to 1300 meters high, all of which were cliffs with several layers, extremely steep. On the ridges of each mountain, the bandits had built several layers of solid fortifications, which could not be penetrated by guns or cannons. Moreover, it was snowing heavily and the cold was piercing to the bone, making transportation difficult. Therefore, the government troops bravely advanced, climbing vines and braving the snow, launching fierce attacks without stopping. The bandits initially did not expect the government troops to have such a desperate and fierce advance, and their morale was greatly discouraged.

Bandit Division Mutinies 113

Just then, Zhang, the commander of the pseudo-Ninth Army (originally defected from a certain unit of the former Hubei Army), saw that the Xu bandit's power was declining day by day, and that the Xu bandit was capricious, fearing that the entire army would disintegrate and that he would not be able to protect himself. Therefore, he changed his attitude and had the intention to surrender. However, the matter was leaked and detected by the Xu bandit, who used the loss of the pass as an excuse, saying that it was due to Zhang's poor performance in combat. He immediately shot Zhang on the spot. Zhang's confidant generals incited the unit to mutiny immediately. The 8th Brigade of the Fifth Route Army took the opportunity to attack forcefully and seized Dadongzhai. Seeing the tense situation, most of the bandits retreated. The 8th Brigade then advanced and occupied various highlands in front of the pass. The Fifth Route Army headquarters received the news and immediately ordered the 7th Brigade to advance and occupy Ciqi Chang from the right wing of Madu Pass, first occupying Chixi Chang and other places. The 9th Brigade advanced and occupied Desheng Chang, all advancing at night and reaching their destinations.

Continuing the Fierce Advance 114

On January 23rd, the 7th Brigade again attacked from the right wing of Madu Pass, occupied Huashiping, Douzui, Foeryan and other places, and continued to pursue. The 8th Brigade occupied Lijia Ping, Madu Pass and other places from the front. The 9th Brigade surrounded and advanced to Daluping, Duanyaping and other places. The Meng Brigade of the 4th Division occupied Qingyun Chang, and the Hao Brigade advanced to Chenjia Ba, Songjia Zui, on the right of the 7th Brigade. The Liao Division advanced to Mao Ba. Seeing the fierce attack of the Fifth Route Army, the Red bandits retreated to Tudibao. The government troops continued to advance and occupied the place. On the morning of the 24th, they continued to chase along the entire line, fighting fiercely until night, occupying Huachishan and Daluping. On the 25th, they continued to occupy Minggu Chang, Zhimuhe, Jiangjia Ba and other places. The bandit army suffered heavy losses in supplies, casualties and injuries. This is the account of the battle of Madu Pass.

Strength of the Bandit Army 115

When the bandit army first came to Sichuan from Shaanxi, they forcibly dragged civilians into becoming bandits, and also dragged more than 500 women and children. The journey took more than three months, and halfway through, the women and children were abandoned or killed in deep valleys. When they arrived in Sichuan, they forcibly formed the farmers of Tongba into the army and fought against the Tian, Yang, and Liu divisions, winning victories. At that time, ammunition was very scarce. After Xuan and Sui, they were replenished with the weapons and ammunition lost by Liu Cunhou, and the military equipment was sufficient. The bandits then considered themselves capable of confronting the Sichuan army. Subsequently, after the main forces of the Fifth Route Army continued to advance and launch four fierce attacks, the bandits suffered heavy casualties. The original veteran bandits and fierce bandits only had a dozen or so people left in each company. The rest were supplemented by guerrillas from Tongba and Xuan Sui. Now each company has only sixty or seventy people. Ammunition is still lacking, with each gun only being distributed with a dozen or so or several rows of bullets. After several defeats, their combat capability has been sharply reduced, and they have been losing ground.

Life of the Bandit Soldiers 116

The reasons for the bandit army's defeat are as described above. In addition, there is another reason, that is, the bandit army manages the troops extremely strictly, killing people at every turn. After finishing the prescribed hard work every day, the bandit soldiers are forced to drill and attend classes, and are forced to receive Red education. If they slightly disobey the orders of their superiors, they are whipped. Each regiment also has a dozen or so children of fourteen or fifteen years old, who are sent to each company to secretly investigate. Those who are not diligent in their work or who talk privately are reported and immediately executed. During combat, they also secretly investigate in the rear, and those who do not advance or retreat are killed without leniency. The officers and soldiers in the bandit army only know how to obey orders and dare not show any displeasure or discuss military affairs. Moreover, the bandit soldiers have only received fifteen strings of Sichuan money in salary for a year. The bandit leaders also know that the amount given is too little to maintain military morale, so they declare that they should only be allowed to eat, not to ask for money. Those who come from other provinces miss their families very much, and those who were dragged from Tongba do not know the whereabouts of their families. The strong resent, and the weak are sad, and can only weep secretly. The stolen silver, food, and clothing are completely transported to the rear. The officers and soldiers in the bandit army dare not ask about it. Therefore, there are many bandit soldiers who want to escape, but they cannot find an opportunity because the surveillance is extremely strict. The mutiny of the entire Zhang Division of the pseudo-Ninth Army the other day was based on this, not accidental. (February 3rd)

Henan Province Launches Widespread Fundraising

To Relief of Hua County Refugees 117

|The Provincial Government Will Commend Those Who Donate 100 Yuan|

Kaifeng Communication: Last summer, the Yellow River flooded, and Hua County suffered heavy disasters. Not only has the accumulated water not receded to this day, but it also suddenly rose four feet on the night of January 12th, and the water poured in with ice, like galloping horses. Forts and embankments were all breached, and many surviving refugees died in the water. Now, men, women, old and young, are mostly floating on the muddy water at night, crying for help. Although various relief agencies and charitable organizations have provided funds one after another, it is a drop in the bucket and does not help. Yesterday, the Provincial Relief Association, in addition to jointly telegraphing the Chairman of the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee, Kong Xiangxi, and the Director of the Disaster Relief Team, Xi Dejiong, to allocate winter relief to save the people's lives, also proposed a one-time widespread fundraising on the Disaster Relief Conference by Zhang Fang, Du Fudong, Yang Zigong, Guo Fangwu, and others. The Provincial Government then issued a notice to all county magistrates to raise funds separately from the first to the seventh day of the lunar new year. Those who donate more than 100 yuan will be commended by the Provincial Government. The details of the method are as follows: "Fundraising Method" Article 1: Each county shall convene government, chamber of commerce, school, local charitable organizations, and gentry to raise funds for seven days. (Now is the lunar new year, when each family is cooking lamb and enjoying the holiday. Everyone should think of the situation of their compatriots in Hua County who lack food and clothing, and are in all kinds of misery, and donate as much as they can.) Article 2: Donations from one copper coin, one sheng of rice or flour, and one set of clothes are all welcome, no matter how much or how little. Those who generously donate a large amount will be reported by the county magistrate to the association, which will forward it to the government for commendation. Article 3: The money, rice, flour, clothes, etc. raised each day shall be kept by the county government in the designated firm or chamber of commerce. After the seven-day period, it shall be reported to the association, which will send someone to receive it together with the local representative, and transport it to Hua County for distribution. Article 4: This method will be decided by the conference and then sent to the Provincial Government's Department of Civil Affairs to notify all counties to implement it. Article 5: Notify those who work outside of Henan, as well as those involved in charitable organizations related to Henan, to jointly bear the responsibility of fundraising and relief. (February 6th)

Funds for Repairing Embankments Have Been Allocated 119

Since the construction of the embankments in the coastal areas of the county, 80% to 90% of the first and second construction groups' projects have been completed. Upon arriving at the scene, he ordered the workers to exhume the coffin from the ground and open it for autopsy. It was found that the deceased, Feng Rongzhen, had a fatal wound on the left side of her head caused by a wooden object, a minor wound on her left arm caused by a wooden object, abrasions on her chest and ribs, and a wound on her left leg caused by a wooden object. The muscles of her buttocks were rotten due to injuries sustained during her lifetime. It was determined that she had died from convulsions the day after being injured during her lifetime. After the autopsy, the body was re-coffined and sealed, pending review and handling.

Ministry of Finance Borrows 130

44 Million Yuan from the Banking Sector

With Italian Refund of Boxer Indemnity as Guarantee

Various Banks Have Started to Disburse the Funds Separately

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the Minister of Finance, Kong Xiangxi, in view of the monthly shortage of military and political expenses, issued 10,000 yuan of customs treasury bills for the 23rd year of the Republic of China to offset the old debts of the Central and other banks. He is now separately conducting new borrowing from Shanghai bankers, with the Italian refund of the Boxer Indemnity to our country as a guarantee. It has now been established, with a total amount of 44 million yuan. The contract has also been signed.

Total Borrowing Amount 131

The total amount of the new borrowing was investigated separately by Xin Sheng News Agency reporters from the leaders of various banks yesterday. It is known that it is indeed 44 million yuan. The rumors of 46 million yuan and 47 million yuan seem to be inaccurate. However, this borrowing was directly contacted by Minister Kong with major banks and did not go through the Banking Association.

Italian Indemnity Guarantee 132

The lending banks are the Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Xingye Bank, Jin City Bank, Dalu Bank, Yanye Bank, Zhongnan Bank, Shanghai Bank, China Industrial Bank, and other more than ten banks, with the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications being the largest, totaling about 20 million yuan. The remaining banks vary, with a minimum of 1 million yuan. The monthly interest rate is 8%, and the Ministry of Finance will repay it in installments until the 37th year of the Republic of China. The Italian refund of the Boxer Indemnity is used as a guarantee.

Starting to Disburse Funds 133

After the banks have determined the loan, they have now started to disburse the funds separately, and it is stipulated that it will be cleared in four months. The Italian refund of the Boxer Indemnity was decided by the former Minister of Finance, Song Ziwen, when he was in Italy, after contacting the Italian government. It is heard that after this loan from the Ministry of Finance is established, the customs treasury bills for the 23rd year of the Republic of China will no longer be mortgaged to the banking sector.

The result is quite satisfactory. The annual interest rate is 6%, and it will be paid off in five years. It is also heard that the contract has been signed last week. The rumor that the interest rate on the loan is 8% per month until the 37th year of the Republic of China, and that it will be paid off, is not true.

Ping-Shanghai Through Train

Accident Occurred in Chuzhou Yesterday Afternoon 135

Wheels Returned to the Track, Continued to Shanghai as Usual

However, Due to Delay, It Will Arrive at 7 AM This Morning

The 301st through train from Ping-Shanghai, which departed from Ping on the afternoon before yesterday at 7:15, was passing through the Chuzhou Station of the Jinpu Railway at 1:30 pm yesterday. Due to the lack of accuracy of the track at the station, a small part of the locomotive fell into the track. The Jinpu Public Works Department rushed to send craftsmen to the scene to lift the wheels and return them to the track, and it was able to continue to run normally. However, it was delayed by nine hours. It crossed the Yangtze River from Xiaguan, and was already at 11 pm. Therefore, the train will arrive in the city at 7 am this morning. Therefore, after receiving the news yesterday, the Beijing-Shanghai Railway immediately advanced the departure of the night train from Beijing to Shanghai at 11 pm, and stopped at each station according to the time of the 301st train, and the 301st train ran according to the time of the night train.

Chen Jiliang's Illness Eases 137

Navy Chief Chen Shaokuan and Others Came to Shanghai Yesterday to Visit

Fever Subsided Slightly Yesterday, Gradually Turning for the Better

Chen Jiliang, Vice Minister of the Navy and Commander of the First Fleet, fell ill in Fujian due to overwork. He took the Hairong ship from Fujian to Shanghai the night before last and was admitted to Renji Hospital for treatment. Yesterday, his condition improved. Navy Minister Chen Shaokuan and Training Fleet Commander Wang Shouting came to Shanghai yesterday morning to visit him. The details are as follows: Navy Chief Chen Visits: Navy Minister Chen Shaokuan learned that Chen was ill in Fujian and immediately telegraphed Chen Cheng, the chief physician of the Shanghai Naval Hospital, to fly to Fujian for diagnosis and treatment. Since Chen has now come to Shanghai for medical treatment, he took the night train from Beijing to Shanghai the night before last at 11 o'clock. Minister Chen only had a few words with Chen because he was extremely exhausted, and then left. Many relatives and friends of Chen visited the hospital yesterday, and all followed the doctor's instructions and did not meet him.

Doctor's Report: Yesterday, according to Chen Cheng, the chief of the Naval Hospital and medical director of Renji Hospital, when the onset of Chen's illness first began, he suddenly felt strange pain in his ribs and waist. Initially, Dr. Wang Zhuozu diagnosed him, some thought that the illness was in his waist, and some thought that it was in the organs or heart. However, because the facilities at the Fuzhou Hospital were too lacking, I was summoned to go there. I arrived in Fujian at about 5 pm on the 5th. After my examination, although I was not able to determine what the disease was, I absolutely believed that it was not the above-mentioned diseases. On the afternoon of the 6th, the symptoms became more dangerous, with a fever as high as 104 degrees, a pulse of 130, and a respiration rate of 40. I then discussed with Commander Li Shijia that if he remained in Fujian, it would be difficult to save him. Commander Li also agreed, but was concerned about the journey. However, in order to emphasize the importance of the illness, he took the risk and took the Hairong ship to Shanghai on the morning of the 7th. On the morning of that day, toxic acids were suddenly discovered in the blood, which was extremely dangerous. Fortunately, with the help of the medical officer and the complete equipment on the ship, he was injected with glucose water and body salt water of up to seven pounds before he was able to escape the danger. Now that these two dangerous periods have passed, I can guarantee that Yu Youren's stroke will gradually recover.

Invite Famous Doctors Lu Zhong'an and Zang Boyong to Treat 138

Apply for Two Weeks of Leave from the Central Government for Careful Recuperation

Yu Youren, President of the Control Yuan, arrived in Shanghai from Beijing the morning before, and suddenly suffered a stroke when he got off the train. His mouth was crooked, and he was mentally confused, which was quite dangerous. After inviting famous doctors Lu Zhong'an and Zang Boyong for diagnosis and treatment one after another, his condition has improved. The details of each situation are as follows:

Banquet for Buddha Unsuccessful 139

According to people around Mr. Yu, the President of the Court, who is currently in Beijing, had originally planned to host a banquet on the evening of the 6th to entertain the Panchen Lama, Zhangjia Hutuktu, and two living Buddhas who had just arrived in Beijing from North China. Invitations were about to be sent out when he suddenly felt unwell, experiencing throbbing in his scalp. Old Illness Returns 140

He then invited the traditional Chinese medicine doctor Lu Zhong'an for diagnosis and treatment. Mr. Yu had suffered from a similar illness in 1928, which gradually healed after medical treatment. Before this recent onset, Mr. Yu's lips were already slightly skewed to the right.

Dr. Zang's Diagnosis 141

According to Dr. Zang's diagnosis, Mr. Yu's blood pressure is not very high. Aside from the crooked mouth and difficulty eating and speaking, his limbs are as flexible as usual, without any hindrance. Therefore, it cannot yet be considered a stroke. However, Mr. Yu is naturally obese, making him very prone to stroke. If he takes good care of himself, it is hoped that there will be no further changes. Mr. Yu's family was initially very anxious, but after Dr. Zang's diagnosis, they felt somewhat relieved. As of last night, Mr. Yu's condition remained unchanged. He was still unable to chew food and was fed small amounts of boiled water and soaked flatbread by attendants.

Two Weeks Leave of Absence 142
