Yesterday morning, Central Committee member Wang Luyi and others went to visit him. Mr. Wang told reporters that Mr. Yu's condition has already improved. For the sake of careful treatment, he has requested a two-week leave of absence from the Central Government.

There is no cause for concern. However, the exact nature of the illness is still uncertain at this time. But he does have a stone in his right flank, which can be determined. Once he recovers his health, he can undergo surgery to have it removed.

Good Progress Yesterday's diagnosis and treatment showed good progress. Yesterday, his temperature was 99.6 degrees in the morning and 98.8 degrees in the afternoon. His pulse was 80 and his respiration was 20. His condition is gradually improving. Currently, Dr. Chen provides daily diagnosis and treatment at the hospital, and it is expected that the effect will be seen day by day. Kong Xiangxi Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday.

Wang Zhengting Returned to Shanghai Yesterday 144

Excellent Feelings about Handling the Aftermath of the Minbian Incident

According to the Central News Agency, the full committee of the Fujian Provincial Government officially took office on the 5th. The Central Party Headquarters and the National Government specially dispatched Central Committee member Wang Zhengting, along with Secretary Fan Guang, to Fujian to supervise the oath-taking. Mr. Wang completed his official duties on the 6th, departed Fujian on the Ninghai warship to Shanghai, and arrived at the Songkou port around 6 PM the previous evening. He disembarked immediately, transferred to a small steamer to enter the port, and landed at the Xinguankou wharf around 9:30 PM, returning directly to his private residence on Route Ghisi. Mr. Wang met with reporters from the Central News Agency yesterday and made the following remarks:

Current Situation in Fujian According to Mr. Wang, after the Minbian Rebellion was suppressed, all the remaining infantry of the 19th Route Army have been reorganized, and Zhangzhou, Quanzhou and other places have also been pacified. The National Army's strategy was swift and admirable. As for the local areas of the province, the upstream areas suffered greatly from this rebellion. The areas near the provincial capital and downstream areas were not significantly affected. However, due to years of disturbance by bandits and the communist party, and the ravaging of local miscellaneous troops, the people's livelihood has been exhausted, and devastation is widespread. At present, the primary task is to restore social order, maintain local security, so that people can live and work in peace, gradually develop transportation, revitalize production, and reorganize finance, which should not be difficult to achieve in order. Currently, the bandit suppression is being carried out actively and effectively, and the highway construction plan is progressing very quickly. The reorganization of disbanded miscellaneous troops is also said to be well-organized. The climate in Fujian is excellent, the products are abundant, and the culture is historically strong. Once organized and the various aftermath measures are in place, one can expect success.

Thoughts on Fujian The most critical issue for China now is the suppression of bandits between Fujian and Jiangxi. When the former 19th Route Army occupied Fujian, they were absolutely unable to implement the bandit suppression. Because while the National Army in Jiangxi was making every effort to encircle and suppress, the Fujian side did not cooperate, and later even reached an agreement with the communist bandits, which further exacerbated the problem. Now that the rebel army has been disbanded, the communist bandits are also in a difficult position. The National Army is now fully cooperating with the various armies in Fujian and Jiangxi provinces to encircle and suppress them. The elimination of the communist bandits is only a matter of time. The recovery of Fujian today, although it is only one province, is actually of great importance to the overall situation and is very gratifying. The northern part of Fujian borders eastern Zhejiang, is mountainous, and rich in forests and agricultural products. Due to the inconvenience of transportation on weekdays, goods are abandoned on the ground, and the local area is extremely poor. After this incident, the authorities felt that the equipment of transportation had a significant relationship with the local area, so they are working on the completion of the highway from northern Fujian to eastern Zhejiang. It is said that the road from Pucheng to Jian'ou can be completed within two months, and the road from Jian'ou to Yanping is also being actively planned, and it is expected to reach Minheng in August. Once this road is completed, the geographical advantages of northern Fujian can be quickly developed, and production can also be transported for export, and northern Fujian can become a fertile and prosperous area. This is really a good sign. Chairman Chen Gongbo has a great deal of experience in military and political affairs, and is willing to take responsibility and be proactive. The directors and committee members of his provincial government are also outstanding individuals of the time, and the future is very promising.

According to the Dagong News Agency, Gu Xinyi, chairman of the Shanghai Bean and Rice Industry Association, telegraphed the Nanjing Rural Reconstruction Committee, Executive Yuan President Wang, and Minister of Finance Kong yesterday, (titles omitted): "The crisis of the collapse of rural areas in our country affects the shake of the national foundation. The rice price plummeted, and it was unable to recover. The people's livelihood was even more painful than before. Recently, it was reported that Japan was dumping large amounts of rice from Korea and Taiwan into our country. Price Reduction for Shanghai-Hankou Through Train Tickets

Only for Direct Trains Between Shanghai, Beijing, and Hankou 147

No Discounts for Intermediate Stations

After the implementation of the Shanghai-Hankou joint transportation through train, the Ministry of Railways, in order to provide preferential treatment to passengers traveling between Shanghai and Hankou, stipulated measures and ordered the railway bureaus to comply. The Beijing-Shanghai, Tianjin-Pukou, Longhai, and Pinghan railway bureaus jointly reviewed and implemented the measures for the joint transportation of passengers between Shanghai and Hankou on the 5th. The first, second, and third-class ticket prices for direct passengers from Shanghai and Nanjing (same as Pukou) to Hankou, and from Hankou to Nanjing (same as Pukou) and Shanghai, shall be calculated at 75% off, regardless of whether it is a one-way or round-trip ticket. No discounts shall be given for other stations. As for the usual round-trip discount ticket prices between stations, they shall still be handled in accordance with the existing regulations. The actual ticket fees received shall be distributed by each railway line according to the proportion of ticket money they should receive. The order was issued quickly and the two railway transportation offices notified each station to comply.

Japanese Merchants Have Already Shipped

Taiwanese Rice Sample Commissioned to Foreign Firms for Sales 148

=Commission and Sales Agreements Have Been Signed and Established=

=Rice Merchants Refuse to Sell Due to the Large Stockpile of Domestic Rice=

=A Portion of Expired Japanese Rice Has Been Shipped to Hong Kong=

According to the Dagong News Agency, the Japanese Osaka Products Co., Ltd. and the Taiwan Colonial Production Bureau have recently shipped more than two million stones of Taiwanese rice to China for dumping. After the samples arrived in Shanghai, they commissioned British and American foreign firms to carry out sales. The rice merchants have all refused. The details are as follows:

Samples Arrived in Shanghai 149

Taiwan, a Japanese colony, produces an average of about eight million stones of rice annually. Due to unfavorable weather last year, the autumn harvest was only 423,109 stones. The rice produced each year is usually transported to Japan and border areas for sales, under the overall planning of the Japanese Ministry of Commerce. This year, the rice stored in Japan is sufficient to meet domestic consumption, and imports are also prohibited in various border areas, resulting in a surplus of more than 3.8 million stones of rice that cannot be sold, and alternative methods must be sought. In addition to 1.6 million stones being transported to the Northeast for sale, there are still more than two million stones that are planned to be transported to our country for dumping. The samples are divided into three grades: first, second, and third class. Mr. Tadata Taro, the representative of Osaka Products Co., Ltd., brought them to Shanghai together with the Taiwan Colonial Production Bureau to find ways to sell them.

Foreign Firms Sales 150

The quality and color of Taiwanese rice are similar to Wuxi rice, the most famous in Jiangsu Province, China. Without the rice industry personnel, it is impossible to distinguish the authenticity. After the rice samples were brought to Shanghai, fearing that direct transactions with Chinese merchants would cause difficulties, the (M.H.D.) American and (L.Q.S.) British foreign firms were specially commissioned to come forward for sales. The commission of the manager and the sales contract have been signed and established.

Rice Merchants Refuse 151

After the managing foreign firm formally established a sales contract with the Japanese side, it sent representatives to the grain industry market for sales. The price was reduced by half a yuan per stone compared to the current domestic rice market. The import duties were all paid by Japan. However, each rice company in the city refused because there was a large stock of domestic rice. According to the person in charge of the rice industry, the current rice price has plummeted, and the suffering of the farmers has accumulated and it is difficult to return. If foreign rice is purchased again, it will create a crisis of rural chaos. The industry has the spirit of love for the country and the nation, and will never make a big mistake to harm the future. Therefore, the foreign firms came forward to sell Japanese Taiwanese rice and have decided to refuse.

Change of Direction 152

After further inquiries from reporters to all parties, the Taiwanese rice, after being refused by the rice industry, the various foreign firms changed their original plan to disappointment, and sent personnel to Guangdong, Guangxi, and Fujian provinces for sales. Also, 25,000 bags of Japanese expired rice stored in Yongxing Warehouse in Lujiazui, Pudong, were transported by Japanese ships to Hong Kong at the end of last year.

New Salt Affairs Measurement System

The Tax Office Said It Would Find a Solution 159

To Ensure That Officials, Merchants and People Are Not Affected

Since the Ministry of Finance decided to issue an order to implement the new measurement system by the Salt Affairs Audit Office, because the weight is nearly 24 catties different per hundred catties compared with the old system, accounting for about one-fourth of the ratio, and when the tax rate was collected, although the Ministry of Finance had studied it once before implementation, in order to make the weight and tax rate of the new and old measurement systems the same proportion, however, the situations in various places are different. Especially in the Lianghuai salt area, since the implementation, the weight and tax rate are very different. After the old system was changed to the new system, the weight difference was one-fourth, and the tax rate was reduced by only one-twentieth. Therefore, after the announcement, they requested the Salt Affairs Audit Office, etc., to reduce the tax rate. A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency went to the Audit Office to inquire about the actual situation yesterday and learned that since the implementation of the new measurement system, the old measurement systems in various places in the past have been uneven, resulting in different collection situations in various places. However, in order to ensure that the people do not increase the burden and the tax revenue is not affected, the Ministry of Finance is now trying to make it balance, so as to ensure that the three parties of officials, merchants, and people are not affected. At present, the Liangzhe salt area has been balanced and there is no problem. However, the Lianghuai prison area still needs to be found a way, and it is hoped that it will be implemented as soon as possible and completely resolved by the Economic Commission.

Moreover, the raw materials for shoemaking, from the silk and呢of the shoe surface to the leather of the sole, and its nail thread, are all subject to customs duties, so although the goods are levied, the tax burden is already high. The Impact of Diesel Tax Increase

Inland Diesel Engine Power Plants Will Be Trapped in Desperation 164

Zhejiang Electric Power Association Has Appealed to the Government

Since the Ministry of Finance began collecting a diesel tariff of 50 yuan per ton on February 1, domestic industrial circles, as well as the electric light and shipping industries, upon hearing this news, were greatly alarmed, as diesel is a necessary fuel for diesel engines, and its selling price is more than 70 yuan per ton. Now, a sudden 70% tariff is levied. The Zhejiang Private Electric Power Industry Federation, located at No. 212 Nanjing Road in this city, finds that electric light companies in Zhejiang Province that use diesel engines to generate electricity account for 89%. Its members require more than 6,000 tons of diesel per year. If the current oil price is maintained, the annual loss will reach more than 300,000 yuan. At this time of popular poverty and commercial difficulties, business is even more difficult, and they will all be forced to shut down. After accepting the requests for relief from representatives of various member companies, the association deeply understands that the electrical industry is closely related to social peace and factory production. Therefore, it has explained the commercial difficulties in detail and submitted requests to the National Government Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Industry, and the Construction Committee, and other agencies, requesting that they withdraw the order and preserve a lifeline for industry. At the same time, the Chairman of the Association, Mr. Li Yanshi, went to Beijing to petition various agencies. It is also heard that various industrial factories in this city are also finding the diesel tax extraordinarily heavy, enough to deliver a death blow. They are appealing to the government separately, striving for a united effort.

Jisheng Association

Jointly Handle the Thatched Shed Fire Incident 167

The Chinese Jisheng Association, due to the fact that there were more than 500 thatched sheds on the barren land of the Yuyuan Road branch of the Shanghai Pudong Nanxiazhe Road Nursing Home, suddenly caught fire at around 11:00 p.m. on the 3rd. Households with the "Zhi" character received six yuan, those with "Ren" received five yuan, and those with "Yong" received four yuan. A total of more than 1,900 yuan in silver dollars was distributed. The police officers dispatched by the area's first district and third division provided care and maintained order. The funds were jointly donated by the two charitable organizations. After the matter was completed, a report was made for record-keeping.

Ningbo Fellow-Villagers Association

Telegraphed Zhejiang Province to Rescue Xu Guangsheng 168

Sentenced to Death for Selling Opium

Xin Xin News reports: The Ningbo Shanghai Fellow-Villagers Association, yesterday, regarding the case of Xu Guangsheng being sentenced to death by the Yin County Court for selling opium, and based on the application for redress from Xu's mother-in-law, telegraphed the Zhejiang Provincial Government and the High Court, stating: "To the respected Zhejiang Provincial Government and High Court of Hangzhou, according to the brief statement of fellow villager Chen Li: 'I am over sixty years old, without children or nephews, few brothers, lonely and helpless, and rely on my son-in-law Xu Guangsheng for a living. On October 24th of last year, Guangsheng was entrusted to carry a small amount of opium from Shanghai to Ningbo. Just as he was about to deliver it, he was suddenly discovered by the Yin County Local Court."

Personnel Dispatched to Investigate 169

"Subsequently, on January 31st of this year, the Yin County Local Court deemed him to be selling opium and sentenced him to death. Guangsheng was ignorant of the law and was fooled by others, which is deserving of punishment. However, to impose the death penalty is inevitably too harsh. The Yin County Local Court cited the Zhejiang Province Regulations for the Elimination of Narcotics. According to Article 5 of the regulations: 'Those who sell or intend to sell and possess or transport opium, red pills, or other narcotics shall be sentenced to death, life imprisonment, or imprisonment of more than ten years. Those whose circumstances are minor shall still be punished in accordance with the Opium Suppression Law.' According to the above regulations, those who are sentenced to death must be in extremely serious circumstances, such that the death penalty is necessary to serve as a warning. If it is due to temporary ignorance or forced by livelihood, then the circumstances are understandable and the situation is pitiful. The responsible authorities may also consider the circumstances and change the sentence to life imprisonment or imprisonment of more than twenty years. Now, Guangsheng rashly carried opium for others due to ignorance of the seriousness of the law, which is not comparable to selling for profit. Even if we take selling as the crime, the circumstances are still minor and should not be"

Punished with the Death Penalty 170

"The Yin County Local Court did not consider the severity of the circumstances and hastily made a final judgment, causing Guangsheng to die unjustly. This is the first point. Moreover, Gong Jinsheng, who was arrested in the same case, had the same criminal circumstances as Guangsheng, but the Yin County Local Court sentenced him to ten years in prison, with different punishments for the same crime. This is the second point. Article 6 of the Provisional Constitution of the Republic of China stipulates that citizens of the Republic of China are equal under the law regardless of gender, race, religion, or class."

Absolutely Equal 171

"The Regulations for the Elimination of Narcotics are a separate law of Zhejiang Province. The rest of the Republic of China, except for Zhejiang, all use the Opium Suppression Law. The penalty for selling opium under the Opium Suppression Law is only imprisonment of one to five years. Under the jurisdiction of the same government, the punishment for the same criminal act is completely different, which violates the provisions of the Provisional Constitution and the principle of the balance of law. This is the third point. Now, the son-in-law, Guangsheng, has"

Violated the Criminal Law 172

"Due to ignorance of the law, and the judges who hold the power of life and death did not consider whether the regulations were lawful or whether Guangsheng's actions were serious, and misused the severe law on a provision that had no right of appeal, resulting in an injustice that cannot be appealed. We ask that the case be transferred for re-examination and rectification, and that an appropriate sentence be imposed to avoid excessive punishment, which is truly a matter of public concern. Ningbo Shanghai Fellow-Villagers Association, Chairman Yu Hede, respectfully."

"Romance of the Fragrant Concubine"

Will Not Cause Turmoil 174

Publishing House Sincerely Accepts Muslim Opinion

Guowen News Agency reports that after receiving a telegram from the Nanchang Muslim Mosque, the Muslim community in Shanghai discovered that the book "Romance of the Fragrant Concubine" contained insulting language towards Islam. They immediately dispatched representatives to seriously negotiate with the publishing house that issued the book. Yesterday, the person in charge of the publishing house stated that they were aware of their mistake and were sincerely willing to accept the opinions of the Muslim community, handing over the remaining copies of "Romance of the Fragrant Concubine" and the printing plates to the Muslim Mosque for public destruction and stopping the sales of the book in branch stores in various ports. According to the Muslim Mosque, if this method is followed, it will not cause turmoil.

Old Newspapers Allowed to Be Charged at Sixth Class 179

The Lianglu Administration received a telegram from the Ministry of Railways yesterday, stating: "According to the Longhai Railway Administration's telegram, 'After checking the grading table, newspapers (bundled) are listed as Class IV, and waste paper is listed as Class VI. However, whether the bundled old newspapers (that is, newspapers that are no longer timely) are charged according to the example of newspapers or waste paper, or should a different grade be set to refine the handling, please telegraph for instructions for compliance,' etc., in addition to replying to the road, it is allowed to compare with the example of waste paper and collect freight at the sixth class, and jointly order all parts to order all stations to comply with the handling. This order has been transferred by the bureau to the traffic department to comply.

January

Industrial Accident Incidents 180

In January, there were 114 industrial and occupational accidents in the Public Concession, injuring 116 people, of whom four died as a result. Thirty people were injured by rotating parts, and four were injured by rotating belts and pulleys. Therefore, it is necessary to install protective devices outside the machinery. There were 12 textile industry accidents, but none were injured by electricity, which may be due to the cold and dryness, which reduces the possibility. In addition, 13 people were injured in construction projects, of which seven fell. There were 16 transportation industry accidents, mostly involving workers on the docks. There were 66 other accidents, the cause of which was not clear.

Municipal Council

Will Ban Large Parades in the Concession 181

The Public Safety Committee of the Municipal Council previously received complaints that large parades in the concession obstructed traffic. The Chief of Police was immediately ordered to discuss solutions. Recently, the Chief of Police submitted a report advocating that the affairs of applying for permits for such parades be transferred from the salary section to the vehicle section, and that the regulations be written in detail in Chinese and English on the permits to restrict them. As for the maximum number of participants in the parade, the committee, after discussion, believed that it should be limited to 300 people. In special circumstances, the Chief of Police may decide on it. Article 62 of the traffic regulations was also proposed to be amended by the Director-General to stipulate that no person may gather, lead, or participate in any parades or gatherings such as weddings or funerals on the road without first obtaining a permit from the Police Department. The Board of Directors raised the case on the 7th of this month and resolved to proceed with it.

Ministry of Industry Instructs Mine Operators

Mine Maps Must Not Use Glossy Paper 182

Starting from March 1, those who fail to comply with the Ministry's order will be rejected. The Ministry of Industry instructed the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday, stating: "It is clearly stipulated in Article 28 of the Implementation Rules of the Mining Law that glossy paper must not be used to make mine area maps, and that orders must not be arbitrarily established, resulting in confusion. However, recently, it has been found that the mine area maps of various provincial and municipal officials and merchants mostly use glossy glass paper for drawing. Not only are the official seals and private seals blurred over time, making them impossible to identify, but also the ink marks on the maps are easily wiped and changed. It is essential to strictly prohibit it in order to enforce the law and prevent abuses. The competent authorities of each province and city should strictly order all mine operators not to use this glossy paper for drawing mine maps in the future, otherwise, they will be rejected. This order will be implemented from March 1. In addition to separate orders, the bureau is ordered to transfer it to all mine operators for compliance. Sincerely,"

Chinese Domestic Cotton Cloth Market in Shanghai

Guiding Production and Improving Products 185

Selecting Basic Weaving Households and Establishing Reward and Punishment Measures

Since its expansion and reorganization last month, the Chinese Domestic Cotton Cloth Market on Guizhou Road in Shanghai has seen a surge in the number of weaving households sending in their cloth. Currently, to provide avenues for weaving households, enhance the skills of weavers, and improve products to promote domestic cotton cloth, the market's Production Guidance Committee has selected those weaving households with outstanding credit and excellent products as basic weaving households. All patterns, sizes, quantities, yarn usage, etc., of the cloth must be woven according to the format separately specified by the market, in order to standardize and facilitate procurement by all parties. It is also reported that reward and punishment measures have been established to provide encouragement. It is hoped that this will create a unique chapter in the history of domestic cloth in Shanghai, allowing it to compete with imported goods.

Spanish Architecture Exhibition 187

Held at the National Hotel in the French Concession starting yesterday

Architect Fan Wenzhao and American architect Lin Peng, recognizing that Spanish-style residences are well-integrated with Chinese living habits and possess the advantages of science and art, and thus have the necessity for promotion, specially consulted Chinese and Western architectural regulations, observed the needs of modern trends, and drafted dozens of the latest Spanish-style residential design plans. Starting yesterday, they are being publicly exhibited for a week at the National Hotel in the French Concession to benefit the contemporary world. Last night, tea and refreshments were provided to the Chinese and Western press in Shanghai, with dozens of reporters from the Continental Daily, China Times, Ta Mei Evening News, North China Daily News, and others in attendance. According to architect Fan, he has been serving in architecture for many years, and he deeply knows the importance of our daily residences, and that improvement without science and art is fruitless. Recognizing that modern Spanish architecture, with its appearance, color, and structure, has much in common with Chinese architecture, we should adopt its values to evoke artistic concepts in our daily residences. Therefore, he is collaborating with architect Lin Peng, who has studied Spanish architecture in the United States for many years, to hold the Spanish exhibition for promotion.

Tong Teh Hospital

Request for Compensation for Self-Built Wards 188

The Tong Teh Hospital and its land at the intersection of Tongfu Road and Dagu Road were originally donated by Huang Cuojiu. Therefore, Tong Teh built operating rooms, clinics, and other facilities on this land, at a cost of about 50,000 yuan. These funds were entirely raised through donations from various sectors. After Huang's death, due to Huang's debt entanglements, the original agreement for the Tong Teh land was overturned and put up for public auction. Tong Teh believes that the repossession of the land has already caused setbacks in public charity and the progress of the highest academic institution, and that being auctioned would lead to complete destruction. Therefore, it has petitioned the court to require the beneficiary to compensate Tong Teh for all the buildings and improvements, so that there can be compensation when building the new school building. Therefore, a certain prominent school director is actively mediating, hoping to achieve the goal.

Dismissed Aide-de-Camp Commits Many Evils 191

Using Military Uniform as Amulet and Using Counterfeit Money

Recently Stealing to Make a Living, Committing Crimes Repeatedly

There is a thief nicknamed "Little Shandong" who has been specializing in stealing items from people's homes in the Putianni Ferry area. He aims to steal anything, including clocks, kerosene stoves, washbasins, foot tubs, stools, chairs, and clothes. His background is that he was an aide-de-camp in a certain former military department, but was dismissed for some reason. He once bought counterfeit money in Shanghai and cashed it in the Jiangbei area. Every time he went, he would return to Shanghai with hundreds of dollars in cash and spend it recklessly. When the money ran out, he would go to Jiangbei again to use his old tricks. However, he deceived Jiangbei merchants several times, and because he was wearing a single uniform, the victims did not dare to argue with him. Later, he was exposed by the local authorities, and the investigation became tighter, so he dared not go there again. However, he stayed in Pudong, unable to make a living, and relied on stealing to make a living. His stealing method is also different from others. During the day, when passing by people's houses, he would enter the house and steal anything at will if he saw that no one was inside. After stealing, he would take the stolen goods to various alleys and sell them at extremely low prices. For example, a self-ringing clock would only be sold for one yuan or a few dimes, a kerosene stove would only be sold for seventy or eighty cents, and so on. Poor people generally bought them cheaply. Seeing that there was a way out, Little Shandong stole more frequently. In the past year or two, countless people have been robbed. Even the day before yesterday, seven families went to the Third District to report losses. Unexpectedly, yesterday, the bandit was suddenly arrested by Detective Li and others from the Third District. In half a day in the afternoon, more than ten families' stolen goods had been recovered. He is currently still being held in the district to continue recovering stolen goods, and will be handed over to the authorities later.

Sentenced for Setting Up Illegal Flower Gambling Listening Post 192

Wu Bingzhou, a Ningbo native, 33 years old, residing at No. 6, Lane 75, Aolihe Road, French Concession, secretly set up an illegal flower gambling listening post at home to collect gambling funds and send them to a large gambling den in Zhabei. Detectives from the French Concession's gambling arrest team found out and rushed to arrest Wu on the afternoon of the 4th, seizing flower gambling slips, gambling fund ledgers, and other items. He was sent to the Second Special District Court, where the police lawyer filed a lawsuit according to law. Wu admitted in the police station that he had only set up the listening post for two days, collecting gambling funds of fifteen to twenty yuan each day and sending them to the Dafu factory opened by Shen Jiafu, Jie Fu, on Changan Road in Zhabei. Unexpectedly, in court, he overturned his previous confession and completely denied it. He was ordered to be detained pending a rescheduled hearing with witnesses. Yesterday, Judge Qiu continued the hearing in Criminal Court Eight. According to the testimony of the landlady, Mrs. Hu, the testimony was very vague, while Wu still insisted on his previous court confession. The court reviewed the confession and found that the evidence of the defendant setting up an illegal listening post was solid, so he was immediately sentenced to one month of imprisonment and a fine of twenty yuan, and the seized evidence was confiscated. The defendant, upon hearing the verdict, declared that he did not accept it and requested an appeal. The court granted it. During the appeal period, he was ordered to provide a surety to be available for summons at any time pending instructions.

Page 13

Child Welfare Association Attention

Child Detention Centers in the North China War Zone 193

Certain Traitorous Countries Ruining Our Country's Children

Currently Engaged in Investigation and Relief Efforts

The Chinese Child Welfare Association has recently received reports from various sources stating that although various agencies have provided relief to various parts of North China after last year's war, the area is still scarred, and the survivors are living in dire straits, lacking food and clothing. Some are even selling their daughters and children to feed themselves. Anyone with a conscience should take steps to rescue them and fulfill the obligation of human mutual assistance. However, it is known that certain countries, disregarding conscience and abandoning humanity, are seizing the opportunity to establish child detention centers under the guise of relief and education at the price of ten or eight yuan, luring poor people to bring their children and daughters into their trap, greedy for immediate petty gains and forgetting the gathering of flesh and blood. Moreover, after the children are detained, the excellent ones are subjected to the destruction of their intelligence, the mediocre ones are subjected to the obstruction of their development, and even, depending on the circumstances, they are arbitrarily slaughtered. Upon hearing this, the association could not help but bristle with anger. Therefore, at the recent meeting of officers, it decided on three measures as relief steps: 1. Communicate and investigate; 2. Publicize the facts; 3. Provide on-site relief. It is reported that the association has already sent out more than a dozen postal and telegraphic messages to solicit information from enthusiastic individuals and organizations in various counties that assisted the association in the North China war zone last year, such as Miyun, Zunhua, Luodong, Changli, Pingtao, Xinglong, Lengkou, Qian'an, etc., to immediately investigate the truth on the ground and report the facts as the basis for the second and third steps of the work.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Asks Guangdong Authorities

To Suppress and Capture the Pirates of Puan and Rescue Passengers 197

Automatic Alarm Motors Installed on Each Ship, Increased Escort Police, Passengers Must Provide Surety

After the Puan ship of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company was robbed, several weeks have passed, but the case has not yet been solved, and the kidnapped hostages are also missing. The company is now actively pursuing the pirates, rescuing the hostages, and implementing anti-theft measures on each sea vessel. The details are described separately as follows:

Commissioner Goes to Guangdong to Handle the Arrest of Thieves 198

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has held several meetings regarding the robbery of the Puan ship, deciding to proceed with the arrest of the thieves and ensure that they are severely punished. Therefore, on the one hand, a large reward was offered to purchase clues to arrest the bandits, and on the other hand, the company specially dispatched Commissioner Sun to Guangdong, carrying the company's reward notices to Guangdong to discuss with the Guangdong provincial authorities practical measures to pursue and arrest the pirates. Because the bandits have entered Guangdong territory, the cooperation of the Guangdong military and police is necessary to solve the case. The most important thing is to rescue the nine kidnapped passengers. The Guangdong authorities have complied with the request of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and dispatched naval and land forces to encircle and suppress the pirates. It is expected that the case will be solved and the hostages will be rescued soon.

Installing Security Automatic Motors 199

The wireless telegraphs on each ship are always located on the highest floor, which is easily trapped by bandits. Now the Ship Affairs Department has drafted an opinion to move the telegraph rooms on each ship to other locations. On the one hand, they are contacting Mr. Xu Zufan of the Security Wireless Telegraph Company, and it has been decided to install the newly invented alarm motor. Once activated, it can generate electricity freely without human power, emitting a signal every two or three minutes. Military vessels within a radius of one hundred nautical miles can receive it and come to the rescue immediately. The company has decided to uniformly add this motor to each sea vessel.

Increasing Maritime Police and Checking and Guaranteeing 200

The escort police on each ship have now been uniformly increased. The original four people have been increased to six people, and Puan has even used twelve people. The number of police has also increased for ships with more passenger seats. Inspectors are assigned to cargo ships. The Fairwind has also discussed adding iron railings. As for checking passengers and obtaining guarantees from passengers introduced by various inns and ticket offices, the Taikoo Company has already implemented it. In order to be cautious about the safety of future voyages and passengers, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will also uniformly follow this procedure to prevent bandits from mixing in.

Puan and English Ship Collision Case

Decided to Submit to Public Arbitration 202

Yesterday, Representatives from Both Sides Inspected the Two Ships and Appointed Experts to Arbitrate Responsibility for the Accident

The Puan ship of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Philoctetes of the British Merchant Blue Funnel Line collided, causing significant losses to both sides. Yesterday, each side sent representatives to inspect the ships, and then scheduled public arbitration. The following is a continuation of the news:

Both Parties Inspect the Ships 203

After the collision between the Puan ship and the Philoctetes, the first important issue was the question of responsibility for the accident. What is right and wrong, and the extent of the damage to both sides, should be publicly verified before repairs can be carried out to avoid further delays. Therefore, yesterday morning, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, together with the Blue Funnel Line, and notified the relevant insurance companies, each sent representatives. The representatives from the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company were Zhao Yuntai and Zhou Houkun, the director and deputy director of the Ship Affairs Department, and engineer Zhao Taibao, the representative of the insurance company. The representatives from the British Merchant side were the manager of the Blue Funnel Line and the representative of the insurance company. In total, there were more than ten people from both sides. Starting at 9:00 AM, they went to Pudong together to publicly inspect the damage to the two ships, which lasted for five hours.

Ascertaining the Damage 204

The representatives of both parties first went to the Blue Funnel Wharf to inspect the British ship Philoctetes. The iron plates on the outer hull of the collision site were all dented. Although the hull was injured, it was not yet broken. After the inspection representatives ascertained the damage, they questioned the shipowners about the incident at that time. Everyone took notes when the shipowners reported. Next, they went to the Chinese Wharf to inspect the Puan ship. They first looked at the damaged part of the bow and then questioned the shipowner, Rex, about the collision, which was very detailed and took a long time. What Rex said was also recorded. After the inspection of the two ships was completed, the representatives returned to Shanghai in the afternoon.

Repairing First 205

The first step of joint inspection has been completed, and the two ships will first enter the dock for repairs to avoid further delays and greater losses to the shipping schedule. Because the cost of each ocean ship, including fuel, is at least seven or eight hundred yuan per day, the damage to the bow of the Puan ship is very serious, and the keel will also be replaced, which will cost a lot. Now the company will have the ship repaired, and the shipyards in Shanghai will submit their bills to the company, and the one with the lowest price and meeting the needs will be selected for repair. Which factory to enter must be decided tomorrow. The Blue Funnel Line's ship will also be repaired in the dock by the company itself, and is currently in contact with various shipyards. The repair of the Puan ship this time will take at least two weeks to complete.

Responsibility Submitted to Public Arbitration 206

It is still difficult to determine the responsibility for the collision between the two ships. Yesterday, the directors of the two ships each had their own arguments. Therefore, it was jointly decided that the two ship companies and the insurance company would jointly appoint several Western members of the ship arbitration committee to form an arbitration office to investigate the case. The reporter also asked Mr. Zhao Yuntai, the director of the Ship Affairs Department of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, who said that the arbitrators have not yet been appointed, but it is likely that the two parties will jointly decide to appoint them tomorrow (the 10th). There are many people in Shanghai who specialize in arbitration, but this case will absolutely not be transferred to the Collision Committee of the Navigation Administration Bureau for handling because the other party is a British ship, which our Navigation Administration Bureau cannot handle, and the Blue Funnel Line also does not agree to be dealt with by the Navigation Administration Bureau.

Prosperity in the South City

Land Prices Soar in the West Gate Area 207

Since the municipal authorities have reorganized the main roads in the Nanshi area of Shanghai, the market has become increasingly prosperous. It is reported that the number of construction projects in Nanshi last year was actually more than in previous years. The area around the east and west gates is particularly lively. Land prices in this area have now risen to nearly 100,000. Traffic at the West Gate is now even more developed. Since the opening of Heping Road, and the extension of the Shanghai Chinese Merchant Tram line to Nanyang Bridge, the daily traffic of cars and horses passing through the area is very complicated. Therefore, the municipal authorities believe that it is necessary to install traffic lights. Construction has been underway since last year for nearly two months and will be completed soon. The municipal authorities are now drafting new traffic rules and will start applying them next month.

Thugs Extort Female Kidnappers

Two Children Rescued 208

Thugs are Guilty, Kidnappers Should Be Severely Punished

Geng Zhangshi, a female kidnapper from Anhui, 41 years old, residing at No. 105 Aixuejin Road, Public Concession, and Zhang Fangshi from Jiangbei, 33 years old, residing at an unknown number on Baoyuan Road, Chinese Concession, took an unnamed four-year-old boy who spoke the local dialect and a six-year-old boy named Lian Xiao who spoke the Tongzhou and northern Anhui dialect to the Jinliyuan Wharf on the Bund in the French Concession on the afternoon of the 7th. They boarded the Tonghua ship of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Shanghai-Shantou route, intending to sell them in Shantou. After the two women took the children off the ship, they happened to meet detectives from the Women and Children Relief Association searching the ship for kidnappers abducting children for export. The two women, feeling guilty, feared being discovered, so they took the children ashore together to temporarily avoid being caught. After the detectives finished searching, they took the children back on the ship. During this process of going ashore and boarding the ship, five or six thugs on the dock saw them. Knowing that the two women were abducting children for export and sale, they followed them ashore and extorted them, demanding fifty dollars. The thugs were also afraid of being discovered by passengers on the ship and people on the dock, so they took the two women and the two children ashore together to the Taixing Hotel on Minquan Road outside Xiaodongmen in the French Concession, opened room 31, and negotiated inside, using soft deception and intimidation. In the end, because the two women had no remaining funds besides the travel expenses they needed, they could not satisfy the thugs' greed, resulting in no results. In the evening, the thugs ordered Li Zhongting (24 years old, residing in Xinkang Lane, Minquan Road), a Ningbo native and companion, to guard the two women and children in the hotel, while they sneaked out to find other ways to achieve their desires. They informed Chinese Constable No. 149 of the French Police Station on duty on the Bund, hoping to find a way. The constable, believing that the female kidnappers taking children abroad for sale involved criminal law, pretended to cooperate with the thugs and told them to return to the hotel and wait, while secretly reporting to the Xiaodongmen Police Station. The police chief immediately dispatched detectives Liu Kunbao and Hu Fusheng to rush to room 31 of the Taixing Hotel, arrested the two female kidnappers and the guarding thug Li Zhongting, and took them and the two children to the police station. Later, the detectives went to arrest the other thugs who were extorting them, but they had all fled. After reporting back to the police chief, Geng Zhangshi was interrogated and admitted to buying the four-year-old boy for forty yuan and taking him to Shantou for sale. Zhang Fangshi claimed that the six-year-old boy, Lian Xiao, was her own son and denied the abduction, but her behavior was inconsistent. Li Zhongting confessed that his accomplices planned to extort the two women. The police chief ordered them to be detained together. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Criminal Court One of the Second Special District Local Court. Judge Wu Fangguang interrogated them. Police lawyer Gu Shouxi stated the case, saying that the defendants were involved in an extortion case, and the police station needed to conduct a detailed investigation and arrest the accomplices who were still at large, requesting a rescheduled hearing. The patrolman then reported the process of arresting the defendants, and the two abducted children were brought to the court. The court asked the children about the abduction, but because they were young, their answers were irrelevant. The judge briefly interrogated the three defendants and ordered them to be detained separately pending further investigation and interrogation at a later date.

This is because the medicine is very effective in treating asthma, asthma, and various lung diseases, and can indeed cure the disease. Therefore, the sales are overwhelming. It is heard that the first and second batches of goods that arrived at the store were sold out within a few days. The third batch of new goods arrived yesterday. Now, major pharmacies in this city and other places are selling it, and the price is the same, still selling for 3 yuan per box. "Accounting" is Selling Well: The editor, Accountant Li, has served as an accounting teacher in various schools in Shanghai for many years and has deep academic knowledge and rich experience. The reprint has now been published, and a large sheet of the Citizen Corps Training Item Examination Table compiled and printed by the society is added. The sales office is Shanghai Printing House, Sande Lane, Ximen, and Shanghai Municipal Yangzheng School, Sanpailou.

Letter 228

In your newspaper on the 4th of this month, on page 14, there was a news item about the cave on Yuntai Mountain collapsing under the pressure of snow, which began by saying that the Shanghai Sealand Joint Transportation Office of Longhai Road received an urgent telegram from Laoyao yesterday, which was very shocking. After checking, this office has not received the above-mentioned urgent telegram, nor has it published the aforementioned news. The content published in your newspaper must be a mistake based on hearsay. After checking, the transfer location for the Sealand Joint Transportation handled by this road and the China Merchants Bureau is Sunjiashan Station. All joint transportation goods are loaded as soon as they arrive, and there are daily telegrams to Shanghai. Since the Hairui Wheel arrived in Sun on the 3rd, more than 2,000 tons have been loaded one after another, which proves that the aforementioned news is not true. We hereby send this letter and ask you to check it and correct it immediately. To the Editorial Department of Shen Bao, Shanghai Joint Transportation Office of Longhai Railway Administration, February 7th.

Reading and Answering Questions

The Usefulness of Dictionaries 229

Reading Guidance:

I currently have a difficult problem, which perhaps many in society sympathize with. Therefore, I dare to raise it, requesting your department to study it.

My command of Chinese is generally adequate for ordinary use, and I believe I have some understanding of scholarly methods and choosing important books to read. However, I am troubled by my lack of English and my unfamiliarity with social science books. When reading new novels, I can only have a vague idea when encountering foreign allusions and terms. Furthermore, there are political science, psychology, and philosophy terms, as well as obscure phrases in classical literature. In these areas, even dictionaries are often unable to provide answers. On the other hand, I lack teachers and friends to ask questions and raise doubts. Therefore, once a doubt arises, it is difficult to resolve.

Explaining such difficult words and phrases might be too trivial, and I imagine it falls outside the scope of your department's guidance. However, the fact remains before me, and if there are few others who feel the same way, then there is no problem; but if there are many, then your department will have to put in the effort to find a solution. It would be best if your department could expand its scope and take on the responsibility of answering difficult words and phrases. If you are too busy to handle it, perhaps you could consider a method and propose it for society's adoption.

I think even for those who are financially well-off, hiring teachers and making friends may be easy, but the categories of these difficult words and phrases are numerous, and one or two teachers and friends may not be able to answer them all completely.

The Textbook Compilation and Review Committee of the Ministry of Education's Elementary and Secondary Schools held a meeting at the Ministry of Education on the afternoon of the 6th from 3:00 to 6:00 p.m. Those present were Ma Ketan, Li Yiting, Wu Shutang, Wu Yanin, Xin Shuzi, Gu Shusen, Wang Jinxin, Xue Tianhan, Pan Pingzhi, Huang Jianzhong, Shen Zishan, Zhu Zilin, and more than ten others. Each period has many large units, and each large unit is further divided into several small units. Because the key points listed in each province and region in the outline still need to be revised, Li Yiting and Wang Jinxin were elected by the public to revise them, and then submitted to the next meeting for decision. "Elementary Society" and "Elementary Nature" have been revised according to the opinions of the Compilation and Translation Bureau, and the work of editing the book is currently underway, which is expected to be completed by the end of February. The Ministry of Education is compiling textbooks. For the elementary school part, the four subjects of Chinese language, arithmetic, society, and nature in the elementary level have all been compiled, and the second step of revision and review is being carried out. For the advanced level, in addition to the above-mentioned history and geography, the compilation outline of Chinese language and arithmetic has been completed but not yet discussed. The Chinese language is entrusted to the affiliated elementary school of Peiping Normal University to compile, and the arithmetic is entrusted to the Suzhou Middle School Practical Elementary School to compile. The advanced nature has been discussed last time and entrusted to the Central University Practical School to compile.

Ministry of Education's Relief

Measures for Diligent and Hardworking Students from the Northeast 235

│Divided into four items, with monthly funding of 27,000 yuan│

(Nanjing, 8th Dispatch) The Ministry of Education has formulated twelve articles of temporary relief measures for diligent and hardworking students from the Northeast, which have been submitted to the Executive Yuan for record. The content of the measures is as follows: The Ministry of Education will set up a Northeast Youth Education Relief Office. The relief matters are temporarily divided into four categories: ㈠ The Ministry of Education will continue to issue a notice to all public and private schools at all levels across the country that diligent and hardworking students from the Northeast, after being verified by the school, will be exempt from tuition fees. ㈡ Those who are truly unable to afford meals, accommodation, books, etc., and who have excellent grades, will be given subsidies separately. ㈢ Establish schools specifically for training students from the Northeast. ㈣ Establish quotas for students from the Northeast studying abroad. Outlying Areas

Various Schools in This City 237

Comply with the School Calendar for Class

The Education Bureau Sends Personnel to Inspect in Different Ways

The Education Bureau of this city has recently found that some private schools do not comply with the school calendar for starting and ending school, resulting in considerable losses for students. For example, if the school holidays are advanced by half a month or delayed by half a month, the students will lose one month of study each semester, which is not a way to rectify the atmosphere of learning. The bureau believes that this matter is of great importance and strictly ordered all schools to comply with the school calendar. It is now known that all schools in this city this semester are able to start school as scheduled. Those who are unable to attend class for unavoidable reasons, such as the two schools of China Vocational and Fudan Affiliated Middle School, due to internships or building school buildings, have all submitted special requests to reschedule classes, which the bureau has reviewed and approved after sending personnel to investigate. Most of the schools that applied for delayed opening, such as Qingxin and other schools, have not been approved, and a quick letter has been sent to teachers and students to start classes earlier. It is heard that the bureau will send a large number of staff to inspect various schools in the coming days in order to enforce the previous order and urge the schools to earnestly rectify.

The City Education Bureau Orders all Private Middle Schools to Submit

The Overall Grades at the Time of Graduation by a Deadline 238

And Retroactively Recognize the Qualifications of Graduates Before Registration

The City Education Bureau specially issued an order yesterday to the private middle schools that have been registered in order to facilitate the retroactive recognition of the qualifications of graduates before registration and to submit the overall grades at the time of graduation by a deadline. The order stated: It has been found that the procedures for registered private secondary schools to request retroactive recognition of the qualifications of graduates before registration and to verify and seal certificates have been stipulated in the eighth and ninth announcements of the Ministry of Education, respectively, and have been notified by this bureau's No. 1795 order to comply with. Now, in order to facilitate the registered private secondary schools to retroactively recognize the qualifications of graduates before registration and verify and seal certificates, the procedures set by the Ministry have been slightly modified for handling. All schools that have submitted the registers of graduates of all previous years as scheduled before April 18 of last year shall submit the overall grades of each subject at the time of graduation of the graduates of all previous years before registration, and fill in the student's academic record card in detail, one for each person, and submit it to the bureau for approval and filing before March 15. The schools may then submit the graduation certificates one after another in accordance with the regulations on the graduation certificates of schools, along with two recent 2.5-inch half-length photos of the person, and request verification and sealing. Others who have not submitted the registers of graduates of all previous years to the bureau by the deadline, or whose reported registers do not conform to the format, as well as newly registered schools, will still handle the procedures for retroactive recognition of the qualifications of their graduates in accordance with the procedures set by the Ministry. In order to review the qualifications of graduates before registration and may review the test papers of each subject at ordinary times and at the time of graduation, check the grades, and order the submission of the admission qualification certificates and other supporting documents of each student. When necessary, the bureau may hold a re-examination on a regular basis. All the previous amendments to the retroactive recognition of the qualifications of graduates before the registration of private secondary schools in the war zone are hereby abolished. This order is hereby issued for compliance.

After the Reorganization of Minli Girls' Middle School

The Opening Ceremony Was Held Yesterday 239

Pan Gongzhan, Wu Xingya, and Others Attended

More Than 600 Teachers, Staff, and Students Attended

Principal Tong Xingbai Presided and Reported

Since the reorganization of the board of directors of Minli Girls' Middle School on Wenmiao Road and the election of Tong Xingbai as the new principal, everything inside has been arranged long ago. The staff has changed very little, and the students are particularly enthusiastic. Yesterday, the school held the spring commencement ceremony, with guests including Jiang Huaisu, representative of the Municipal Party Department, Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Education Bureau, and school board members Wu Xingya, Yang Weiyu, Wang Yansong, Zhu Xinong, and more than 600 teachers, staff, and students, which was quite a grand occasion. Chairman Tong Xingbai presided over the ceremony. First, the chairman reported, saying that everyone has a kind of nervous emotion and enthusiastic state at the spring commencement ceremony of our school today, which has never happened before. Generally, after the reorganization of our school, what will be the impact on the future of teachers, staff, and students, and what is my attitude and proposition for running the school are urgently to be made clear, so I have to explain to you first. First, I am willing to be a good friend of Minli Girls' Middle School. The past advantages of our school should not only be retained, but also be promoted. The past shortcomings must also be improved to be perfect. All the students and teachers love our school, so my position is exactly the same as that of my brothers. Since the positions are the same, we should work together to seek the progress of school affairs. Secondly, my brothers came here to serve the main club purely, because the school is a social group, education is a national policy, and private schools are just educational undertakings run by the people, which are completely different from the nature of private property. Since the nature is clear, a clear understanding of this reorganization can be obtained. Again, my brothers have always held a view on things, that is, to do things and never to people. To be able to do things and do them well is a good thing. Those who do good things are good people. We can't ask for good people, so how can we let him idle? So we only ask whether things are done well, regardless of whether people are different or not. The above three points are clear, and we can understand each other, and all actions can proceed smoothly, which is of great benefit to the development of the school. In addition, as for what kind of policy should be adopted in the school's education and training, because the scope is too large, it cannot be fully described in a few words. However, seeing the current cultural crisis in China, I feel that girls' education in the future should create a kind of hard-working and striving news discipline to save the general youth's decadence and romantic enjoyment. Therefore, the school's education and training policy in the future should proceed in this direction. Secondly, Jiang Huaisu and Pan Gongzhan gave speeches successively, with many encouraging words. Finally, because Chairman Wu Xingya was not feeling well, school board member Yang Weiyu gave a speech on behalf of him, and then the ceremony was over.

The First Vocational Supplementary School of the Vocational Education Society The First Vocational Supplementary School attached to the Chinese Vocational Education Society on Hualong Road in this city has achieved remarkable results since its establishment. The number of people in each subject has increased year by year. Starting from the next semester, it will be expanded and there will be more subjects. In addition to English, Japanese, Bookkeeping and Accounting, Documents and Statistics, Chinese, Advertising Painting, Arithmetic, and Chinese Typing, a preparatory course for further studies, a Chinese shorthand course, and an English business translation course will be added. Experts are invited to teach all courses. Recently, those who have been requesting prospectuses and registering have been very enthusiastic.

Huadong Girls' Middle School on Beile Road in this city opened on the 1st of this month and has officially started classes. Chinese Basketball Court is Full

Maklin Defeats Zhanghua in the Group B Final 257

74-51 Zhanghua, though strong, can only hold out for five minutes.

Maklin's performance is unexpectedly wonderful.

The Pirates have won the Group A championship.

The Shanghai basketball Group B final between Zhanghua and Maklin was held last night at the Chinese basketball court surrounded by over a thousand spectators. Maklin's performance was magical. Zhanghua only had a slight advantage in the first five minutes. After that, they were defeated and unable to control the situation. Maklin was tall, agile, with excellent passing, and especially accurate shooting. Zhanghua's Qian Jingyong had accurate vision, but his shots were not opportune. They were behind 22-41 in the first half, and the total result was 74-51. The Pirates have completed the Group A order. Yesterday they defeated the Jews easily and will wait for the Group B winner to compete for the championship.

Wonderful Performance 258

The first five minutes of the performance were full of wonderful moments. Zhanghua went all out, with an overwhelming momentum, and seemed invincible. They were very well coordinated and creatively won. But after 12-12, Maklin suddenly rose sharply and was unstoppable. Zhanghua's defense could not contain its momentum. Sun Baoqing was too short, Lu Zhongen could not take care of everyone, and Chen Xianglong repeatedly allowed Locke to sneak in, creating a surging tide. The ball went to the enemy's hand and was instantly at the basket. Three forwards surrounded it, and nineteen shots were made. Zhanghua's Chen Xianglong ran slower, and it was difficult to cooperate with Feng Qian. Moreover, they could not win the jump balls in the middle, so the momentum of the ball was always at a disadvantage.

Golden Age 259

After Lu Zhongen opened the scoring in the first half, he committed two fouls in a row, and he could not help but feel anxious. At the same time, Maklin's Bie Xupo also committed two fouls in a row, which was a coincidence. Mou Lei penalized Lu Zhongen, and Qian Jingyong penalized Bie Xupo, each adding one point, making it 3-1. Le Ai scored to make it 3-3. Maklin called a timeout, and Bie Xupo attacked from the rear, adding two points. Maklin then took the lead at 5-3. Lu Zhongen advanced and coordinated, and made a wonderful shot six yards in front of the basket. Qian Jingyong made two corner shots, which were extraordinary, making it 9-5, Zhanghua's golden age. The performance was so good that it was worth seeing.

Gradually Balancing 260

Maklin's momentum gradually rose, with an aggressive attitude. Zhanghua suffered greatly due to the disadvantage of jump balls in the middle. Initially, Chen Xianglong blocked Locke's shot, but the ball was hit and he was penalized again, losing three points to make it 9-8. Qian Jingyong scored again, and Chen Xianglong added one point, making it 12-8, still taking the lead. Bie Xupo made two long shots ten yards in front of the basket, making it 12-12. From then on, Zhanghua's golden age passed. The previous persistence and struggle of Zhanghua, which repeatedly took the lead, was because the defense was still able to contain the enemy's attack.

The Good Times Are Gone 261

The flowers are not always in bloom, and the good times are gone. Zhanghua's strategy has not changed. Lu Zhongen still goes forward to assist the forwards, causing the rear to be empty. When the shots are missed, and the ball falls into the hands of the enemy, Maklin's two forwards have already sprinted to the basket. Zhanghua could not return in time, so the ball was lost one after another. Maklin continuously increased their score by ten points. Feng Nianhua opened his personal record. Locke shot with both left and right hands, and was able to shoot from any position. From then on, the situation was very different. Zhanghua was twice as far behind in scoring. In the first half, Maklin scored 41 points, and Zhanghua scored 21 points.

The Situation Is Disparate 262

As the battle started again, Feng Nianhua gradually began to show promise. Maklin's Le Ai and Bie Xupo retreated and were replaced by Boris and Ge Lak. Boris made two shots out of two. Zhanghua tried to struggle. Feng Nianhua was much more active than in the first half, making two consecutive shots. Qian Jingyong also added one point. His technique and vision were very skilled and accurate. Three consecutive shots. In less than a minute, the situation seemed to be improving again, 30-45, a difference of fifteen points. But in reality, it was difficult. Moreover, Maklin's momentum had not diminished. In a moment, Boris and Mou Lei added ten points again. From then on, Zhanghua was often behind by more than twenty points.

The Trend Has Been Determined 263

The situation became a torrent, and the situation was determined. Maklin still deployed troops from time to time, and Zhanghua also rose and fell from time to time. They once scored eight points in a row, but the gains did not make up for the losses, 38-56, a difference of eighteen points. Locke and Mou Lei added icing on the cake, making it 66-38, a difference of 28 points. After that, the situation gradually declined, and the audience scattered like birds and beasts, and the scene was chaotic. Zhanghua made a final struggle, adding up to 51 points, while Maklin had 74 points. Then the time ended.

Getting What They Deserve 264

Zhanghua's defeat was not expected to be so many points lost. However, Zhanghua's performance was still beautiful. What was lacking was that the running and passing was still too slow. Maklin's victory has its own special techniques. Zhanghua is still far behind. The reason why the Western Youth Basketball Pirates lost to Maklin was that the court was too small, not enough for Maklin's activities. Now that Zhanghua has been defeated, Maklin can win the Group B championship. In the future, when Maklin and the Pirates meet again, the Pirates will find the court too large and unable to use their skills. Maklin will win the championship.
